電影專刊

中華民國貳拾貳年壹月貳拾叄日星期壹（不另取　）

好萊塢的經濟危機 256

— 福倫

本刋及其他電影刋物裏，提到好萊塢的富庶奢移，似乎都欣欣樂道的，所以給與讀者的一斑印像，就是滿地鋪金，白玉砌墻，銀灰色的律摩心毫無聲息地飄來飄去，裏面坐的是神仙眷屬。其實，現在却已不似從前了。所以爲解除讀者過分的崇仰心，實有介紹這篇文字的必要。

好萊塢新聞記者寗娜普南女士說，好萊塢的内容，有不可究詰的　衷，但是外表仍舊硬裝塲面，不肯坍臺。法國的大影評家某亦於日前發出驚人的預言，說好萊塢於六個月之内，仍發生經濟及藝術的大崩潰，可以使全世界震驚。我們雖不能一定相信好萊塢在最近半年内，將一蹶不振，但至少可以對於這種預示，說一聲[不爲無因]吧。

寗娜女士曾訪問過一位好萊塢的大明星。他仍舊住在皮佛山上最富麗一所房子裏。好進去的時候，正値主人們進膳。她看見檯上羅列的食品，似乎不大豐富，但是她還是不大在意。她後來看見屋子内沒有電燈，點的係蠟燭，她慢慢有些異起來了。但是主人說他的太不喜歡幽靜，所以不開電燈的。後來她乘主人一個冷不防　溜到别間屋裏，開開電門，亦沒有電。她恍然大悟了，並且起了一種悚然的恐懼。呀，世界的不景氣，居然侵入了這金吾不夜歌舞未央的影城了！她又一個　入地蔭子（地下層，裏面專爲煤爐，片鍋，烹飪之所），劃了一根洋火，發見煤氣灶上煤氣亦沒有了。給她發現的事情很多，這位大明星的住宅裏，非但電燈煤氣都已割斷，連電話亦不通了。

但是他仍舊不能不照樣的住在這所大房子裏，硬挺頭皮，仍舊要坐富麗的大汽車；遇見人家問［您好？］的時候，仍舊要硬撑塲面地說［很好，謝謝您。因爲他倘使不如此，他馬上就要被人家看不起，就要站不住脚，祇好捲舗蓋滾蛋。

受同樣影響的當然不止他一個。許多銀行關門了，各種投資失敗了，明星們昔日冰山有靠的，現在已經一貧如洗，從前他們可以和廠主導演閙脾氣，一來就慣紗帽不幹，現在祇好低心下氣地尋些隨便甚麽事做做，有許多本年沒事可做，却不肯承認失業，而要每天坐了汽車，停在大公司的門口，或向攝影塲裏去轉一轉身。嗐，這多苦，而可憐呀！

海外珍聞

影界二個新發明 257

— 興之

美國加州近來新造一個大戲院，是二個戲院合成的，戲台在中間，當開映的時候，二邊都可以入座觀看，這樣一來，可以使坐位寬舒些，不至過於擁擠，以一個戲台而兼施二個戲院的職務，也可以算别開生面，發明者是一個美國工程師，計畫了許久，到現在才實現。

德國有一個工科大學的敎授，發明一種光學器械，在戲院中影戲開映的時候，可以隨手在這架機器的玻瑙片上冩字，一面寫一面就在銀幕上放映出來，對於報告臨時消息，時事緊要新聞和名人留筆等，都有種種便利。這位敎授發明之初，是利有做一個大課堂上敎授數學中極繁重的方式，的很來才用到戲院裏去，現在已有不少戲院採用了。

［明星］的製片新計劃 258

— 青霞

明星公司的製片廠雖沒有聯華那麽多，但在去年的出品總數，似乎不出聯華之下。不過他們對於在拍攝每一部影片之前，並不限定此片最多用多少尺的底片；如［啼笑姻緣；］［自由之花；］····等片，這都是化去三萬餘尺的底片才得到一萬尺左右的影片：而一部七八千尺的影片，用掉兩萬多尺的底片，更是占着他們出品中的多數。所以他們每年所用的底片總數，總是超乎任何那個公司之外。他們覺得長此以往，殊不是善策，很想卽刻實行節省；可是他們爲欲使出品美滿，終於不敢遽然實行。這也使他們萬分的艱難。

最近鄭正秋因爲這個問題曾和公司中重要職員如周劍雲等一度討論改善辦法；當時議决縮短影片尺數，並增攝［卡通畫。］名畫家萬籟鳴·萬古蟾兩君之人明星，就是被聘爲擔任［卡通畫］主任。

［神秘的小偵探，］就是現在剛開拍的［卡通畫，］演員有譯志遠·張敏等；片長一千尺。因爲此後明星的出品，較嚋昔的爲短，故這種［卡通畫，］是預備將來隨着正片開映的。

天一公司的女童星之羣伶 259

— 央

在目下中國電影界，對於童星的缺乏，和需求之迫切，是誰也不能否認的事實。因此，這孕育·在天一公司裏的女童星之羣，實在是値得我們注意的啊！這裏，記者特把這一羣女童星介紹出來：

袁美雲：她在未從事電影工作之前，是一個著名的舞台小女伶，她有嬌小玲瓏的身叚，活潑伶俐的姿態，更富有表演的天才，她在目下的中國電影界裏面，可以算是天字第一號的女童星哩！

邵素霞：好是天一的協理邵邨人的女公子，今年十四歲，在市立比德小學讀書，天眞爛漫，會唱歌·會彈琴：好像一隻活潑的小鳥。她在默片時代，已做過不少部影片的要角·有聲片［游藝大會］及［戰地］［孤女］她也參加在人。在新片［孼海雙鴛］中，她飾一個被窮人撫養的富翁的女兒，表演得很好。

陳綺霞：！是天一公司老板娘陳玉梅的妹妹，活潑天眞，在［游藝大會］中的載歌載舞，留下非常好的成績，給人一個好印象。預料將來必有更驚人的成績，貢獻出來。

陳競芳：她的年紀雖小，却已長成的像一朶芙蓉般的鮮艶了。她在［蘭谷萍踪］中飾一個婢女，獲得佳譽，更有人說她的成功，不下於陳燕燕的［一剪梅］哩。我們期望她今後更加努力，成爲一顆名童星。

瓊克勞馥的化裝警吾 260

瓊克勞馥，葛蘭泰嘉寳·瑙瑪希拉·這是美高梅公司的三大台柱，爲了各人有各人的藝術，各人有各人的觀衆，所以不絶的前進，想奪取美高梅的寳座，葛蘭泰嘉寳伏她的神秘魄力，終於奪取了這寳座，於是野心勃勃的瓊克勞馥便鈎心鬥角地各嘉寳對抗，想從嘉寳手裏把寳座奪來，現在嘉寳已回她的故國瑞典去了，美高梅的寳座也就爲瓊克勞馥所取，但是觀衆之擁嘉寳的心，并不因此而稍懈，我們這聰明的瓊克勞馥，又要想把觀衆擁嘉寳的心轉過來擁護她，這只有用仿模的法子，所以她近來化裝，也仿模嘉寳，想博得觀衆的歡迎，我們等着將來在她所主演的［雨］一片裏ＴｈｅＲａｉｎ，就可以看見她的化裝有點神秘了，那兩片的朱唇，眞是够人肉感，但是牠雖然這樣的化裝，可是却很關心觀衆對於她改變作風的批評，惟恐觀衆對她這樣的化裝發生反感，致失去她的寳座，所以她近來很關心觀衆的心理呢。

電影與文學趣味 261

— 黃震遐

㈡晚安維也納

中歐羅巴十九世紀的風情，中歐羅已十九世紀的文化。

維也納，這德奥民族的故都北平，由藍色的多腦河環流着，在十九世紀初葉，古堡森嚴，圓舞曲的旋律輕浮於細草之上。他是中歐最古之城，神聖羅馬帝國的帝都，天才音樂家的搖籃地，而爲羅曼情趣的集中點，我們在名畫中所見到的古典派美人，長裙拂地，臉上點一顆很大的黑痣，以及那些寳刀駿馬的武士，卽所謂日爾曼藍十字騎士，豪俠之風，結晶而成這中古羅曼的文化，而由貝多芬許貝德等用天堂的音響幻化其氛圍，降至近代，其在歐洲藝術上地位，仍佔最優秀地位丨丨［晚安，維也納，］便是以這［夢幻之都］爲背境的一張音樂喜劇，所謂［晚安，維也納］者，便是一位近代騎士，對這［夢幻之都］徬於征途上所發出的戀别呼聲，其凄艶之情緒，實與拜倫告别英國時的［晚安，我的故響］異曲同工。全片的結構趣味豐饒，極温馨美麗之至，可稱爲西洋音樂藝術精髓的副產物。其對於人生的態度，是反對嚴肅化的活潑小諷刺，但仍不脫中古騎士少女的羅曼作風，如男主角必須爲軍官，女主角必須先爲賣花女，後爲著名女伶是。

總之，影片就是烘托給我們以維也納的夢之美麗，及其美麗的人物，這純是文藝的副產物，是反對把人生變成嚴肅認眞化的調劑品，很有點巴黎風的幽默態度，若以時髦政治眼光視之，則維也納旣爲歐洲封建勢力的發源地，劇中人物又無不極端地小資產階級劣根化，絲毫也不革命、自然祇是［流毒的麻醉品］。

介紹霓裳仙子 262

— 羅拔高

德國烏發影片公司在世界影壇上是站着超然的地位。它的出品，不管是甚麽一種題材，都是聚精會神，全力奔赴，絲毫地不肯苟且。我們從它那［斬龍遇仙記］一直數到現在在南京大戲院開映的［龍翔鳳舞］，有那一張不是在適合於電影藝術的條件上而給予觀者以美妙良好的印象？

據說［霓裳仙子，］是烏發公司去年出品上乘與［龍翔鳳舞］並駕齊驅。在歐州各都會，同亨盛名。［龍翔鳳舞］是音樂歌劇化，［霓裳仙子］也是音樂歌劇化，不過題材不同，導演的手段不同。除此之外［霓裳仙子］的劇材幽默化，是一種人生的小諷刺。

全劇的描寫非常輕飄，冷雋，有巴黎風。拿一個小國度來尋開心，甚爲幽默。然而它寫的是一段夢幻般的人生，快樂甜蜜，屈服於戀愛至上主義之下成了青年男女們的憧憬。

它的題旨是以小來喻大的，對於君主政體有絶對的懷疑，它挖苦官僚政客武人，它搶白豪商鉅賈，它譏誚屬僚部員，它却同情於生命之火的燃燒，青春的活躍。

它的英文名Ｒｏｎｎｇ不日將在新光開映。

四郎探母之成績 263

— 趙虎

古代有聲影業公司出品，尹聲濤導演，名伶雪艶琴譚富英主演之全部四郎探母，業已拍攝完竣，雪艶琴譚富英皆係舞台上之名角，拍攝有聲電影，尙屬初次，而表演之佳，一如老練之電影明星，誠難能而可貴也。

當拍攝該片之初。對於劇中之佈景等，煞費苦心，尤以蕭太后之皇宫花園，富麗堂皇，皆非觀衆所能常見者。

四郎探母在銀幕上，演來確比舞台上更妙，蓋有偉大之佈景，爲之點綴，就中以人馬論，亦比舞台上多出數倍，所以在銀幕上之四郎探母，實足使觀衆爲之滿意。

［四郎探母］中之一幕 264

［火柴大王］本事（十七） 265

— 希孟譯

在這裏，他自己創造了森羅地獄，但也是在這裏，他自己跌入了那自己創造的森羅地鉃，和其他先跌入這森羅地獄的，同歸於盡。

那意大利國庫券係假造的，現在發現了。四千萬元的轉賬亦取銷了。四面陰雲慘合，天羅地網，蓋將下來，保羅克魯爾，愛立克，以及其他一切同事，都逃不了，身敗名裂。監牢的門，開直了等候他們的蒞臨。

紐約，倫敦，柏林，巴黎，世界各處的交易所，都岌岌欲倒，發出天崩地坼的聲音出來許多國的内閣倒了，許多國的政府推翻了。革命各處發生。人心惶惶，不可終日。

保羅回到公事房，聽見了衆人的咒咀，眞是上天無梯，入地無門，悄悄地逃走了。他一個人坐在寫字檯上，在那裏想，他承認這回的失敗，是無法可逃的了。他一時心血來潮起來。

以前的所往所歴，都一一回到心頭，如漩渦似的急轉，似電影裏的一幕一幕，重現於眼前。

似小說似的，因果相乘，結局如何，他早已了了於心，無所容其逃避。

最後，他開了他的秘密保險櫃，取了一支手槍放在衣袋裏。他很敏捷地離開了他的公事房，走到陽台上。他一陣一陣地想起以往之事，從美國芝加哥受他排擠去職的清首夫起，一直到慕爾娜告訴他，她已經愛了别人爲止丨丨那一帮受過他害的人，一個一個地站立在他的面前丨丨蓓蓓，桑尼亞，羅定斯基，那位老發明家，斯加拉底，各國的銀行家，政治家，財政家····他眼睛突然地發出一種可怖的兇𦦨。他舉起手槍，對住了他自己的太陽穴黑夜迷濛之中，但見橘黃色的火光一亮，他已經從陽台上滾過欄干，跌在街上。

許多人，聽見了槍聲，追到他的公事房從公事房追到陽台。他們望下面一望，都　　了大家拚命似的奔向電梯。

在樓下街上，他們看見了他的屍體，各人心中有各人的感想。

保羅的身體，躺在陰溝裏，他的頭撞在一個清道夫的兩輪車的車輪上。他脚跟的旁邊，堆了一堆燒過的火柴，愛立克最後自言自語地說：

［他是從掏陰溝出身的，丨丨他從陰溝裏上升一直到控制全世界丨丨他還是死在陰溝裏。］

（完）

1933.01.23

Today's Main Points of This Newspaper 1

Domestic: Luo Wen'gan Publishes Remarks Refuting Uchida's Absurd Speech; Traitor Zhang Jinghui Plans to Invade Jehol from Suizhong; Duan Qirui Arrives in Beijing; Various Circles Commemorate the Fallen Soldiers at Yuguan.

International: League of Nations General Assembly to be Convened Early Next Month; Rumors of Instability in Japan's Saito Cabinet; Herriot Issues Declaration Advocating Cooperation Between Britain, America, and France.

Shanghai: Citywide Labor Representatives Hold Congress; Commemoration of January 28th Incident; Municipal Federation Advocates One-Meal Frugality on the Anniversary; American News Reporter Vincent Arrives in Shanghai.

Mediation Procedures Appear Hopeless, League of Nations Still Awaits a Turning Point 2

The Nineteenth National Congress Will Continue This Morning to Discuss Methods for Drafting a Report

Japan Maintains a Consistently Tough Stance, Threatening to Withdraw from the League

Special General Assembly to Be Convened Early Next Month 3

(Geneva) The Committee of Nineteen Nations, in view of the failure of mediation procedures, decided to draft a report in accordance with Article 15, Paragraph 4 of the Covenant. This matter was decided after the committee discussed it for two and a half hours yesterday. The united front of the Committee of Nineteen Nations will be maintained to the end, and it is unwilling to change the resolution adopted on December 15 of last year. Chairman Hymans reviewed the recent proposals of China and Japan and felt that Japan only recognized what was beneficial to it in the methods proposed by the Committee of Nineteen Nations on Wednesday, i.e., not allowing non-member states to participate. In addition, Japan has various demands that are contrary to the spirit and wording of the December 15 resolution, the most important of which is the demand to delete all words related to "Manchukuo" in the preamble and the resolution itself. Also, if the current procedures succeed, the tasks of the mediation committee are to be limited. This is the position of Japan. As for the demands put forward by the Chinese delegation, namely, not recognizing "Manchukuo" and inviting the United States and Russia to participate in the discussions, the positions of the two sides are so different that the Committee of Nineteen Nations cannot but recognize the failure of its efforts. In the future, there will be only one method: drafting recommendations without the participation of the two parties involved. However, only the Special General Assembly of the League of Nations has the power to formally certify the failure of the mediation procedures. The above remarks by the Committee of Nineteen Nations do not represent a decision on behalf of the General Assembly. The Committee of Nineteen Nations is scheduled to meet on Monday to draft the first report, so as to report the negative results of its efforts to the Extraordinary General Assembly. It is generally expected that the Extraordinary General Assembly will be convened in early February to make a final decision on the proposals of the Committee of Nineteen Nations. When the Extraordinary General Assembly convenes for the second time, it will, in accordance with Article 15 of the Covenant, review the recommendations drafted by the Committee of Nineteen Nations. This is the committee's second report. (Havas dispatch from Geneva, 22nd)

(Geneva) The Secretariat of the League of Nations published the original text of the two draft resolutions and explanatory memorandum sent to the Chinese and Japanese delegations on December 15. (Reuters dispatch from Geneva, 22nd)

Acknowledging Mediation Failure, Preparing to Draft a Report 4

(Geneva) The Nineteenth Special Committee met at 4:00 PM on the 21st for two hours and fifteen minutes, deciding that mediation procedures had almost failed and discussing procedures for drafting a report on the dispute as outlined in Article 15, Paragraph 4 of the Covenant. Finally, it was agreed to adjourn until Monday morning to continue the discussion, and at the same time, three draft proposals of this report will be sent to the members of the Nineteenth Special Committee. The content is currently kept secret. The Special Committee has not yet abandoned the possibility of mediation. If any of the two parties puts forward a new proposal that can form the basis for a resolution, the Special Committee will welcome it.

British-Japanese Compromise Plan, Drummond Strenuously Clears Himself 5

Today, the Special Committee studied the Japanese proposal and unanimously decided that several points were absolutely unacceptable. Therefore, it unanimously decided to proceed to the second stage. Secretary-General Drummond attended to explain the so-called Drummond plan. The Special Committee found Drummond's explanation satisfactory and decided to bring the matter to a close. The Special Committee felt that the opinions of China and Japan were too far apart, and mediation seemed unlikely.

Special Session Continues This Morning, General Assembly Convened Early Next Month 6

The Swiss representative, Mr. Huber, declared that only the League of Nations General Assembly can decide whether mediation has failed. Therefore, the Special Committee decided to leave room for mediation before the League of Nations General Assembly convenes, while proceeding with the drafting of the report. It is expected that the League of Nations General Assembly will convene on February 1st or 2nd. One member raised the question of whether the drafting of the report should be discussed with the League of Nations General Assembly, but the members believed that, according to the duties of the Special Committee as stipulated in the resolution of March 11, 1932, the Special Committee could proceed with the drafting of the report. The Special Committee continued to discuss methods for a considerable amount of time and decided to continue the discussion at 10:00 AM on Monday morning. The content of the report has not yet been discussed, and it may not be discussed even on Monday. The Executive Yuan originally scheduled a meeting for next Monday, but because the Special Committee is meeting that day, the Executive Yuan meeting has been postponed to Tuesday.

Public Communiqué Issued at the Meeting, Welcoming New Proposals from Both Sides 7

The communiqué issued after today's meeting is as follows: At the afternoon meeting today, the Special Committee learned from the declaration made by the Japanese representative to the chairman and secretary-general that the Japanese government is not prepared to accept the draft resolution of December 15, even if the section inviting non-member states to participate in the negotiations is deleted. After issuing this declaration, the Japanese delegation informed the chairman that the proposal automatically submitted to the Special Committee by the Japanese representative yesterday had been approved by the Japanese government. After studying the new proposals of the Japanese government and the Chinese amendments to the original text of the draft resolution, the Special Committee has notified both parties that it can only declare that it cannot put forward a proposal acceptable to both parties. If the Special Committee must also modify other conditions of the December 15 draft resolution according to the Japanese proposal, the importance that the Chinese delegation and the Special Committee itself attach to the participation of the United States and Russia in the settlement negotiations will definitely make it impossible to delete this section merely at the request of the Japanese side. The Special Committee also felt that even if it was agreed to change the explanatory memorandum into a declaration by the chairman of the Special Committee, so that both parties could freely make reservations, the Japanese government would still have to wait for the original text of the December 15 draft resolution to be modified before it could accept it. The Japanese government has requested important modifications to the original text of the Special Committee's draft resolution in its recent proposal, which the Special Committee considers unacceptable. Under these circumstances, the Special Committee feels that the effort to propose reconciliation of the dispute to the League of Nations General Assembly has, as far as the Special Committee is concerned, temporarily failed. The Special Committee has to assume that the League of Nations General Assembly will have the same result at its next meeting. Therefore, in accordance with the mission of the Special Committee as stated in Section 3 of Article 5 of the March 11 resolution, it has decided to begin compiling the draft report stipulated in Article 15, Paragraph 4 of the Covenant. As for the procedures under Article 15, Paragraph 3 of the Covenant, only the League of Nations General Assembly can conclude them. Therefore, the Special Committee is of course prepared to welcome any new suggestions that the two parties are willing to put forward.

League of Nations Has Fallen in Prestige, Fourteen Months of Work Have Been Unsuccessful 8

Today's situation is still far from resolution and has made no progress compared to fourteen months ago. The members are indeed eager to end this fruitless scene, but several members of the Nineteenth Special Committee, including those who most strongly advocate maintaining the League of Nations Covenant, are now proceeding cautiously, fearing that one wrong step will lead to a fall into a dangerous cliff. This is an unprecedented situation, with no precedent to follow. Therefore, the Special Committee often engages in time-consuming and fruitless debates, such as the confusion encountered today over whether the Special Committee has the right to declare the failure of mediation and begin drafting a report. The above-mentioned dispute has been resolved in two ways: (1) Deciding to keep the mediation path nominally open, and (2) Deciding to draft a report and ask the League of Nations General Assembly to pass it. Rumors are now circulating that individuals or small groups within the Nineteenth Special Committee want to propose draft proposals that differ from each other, but each member, in private interviews, said that unity and caution should not be taken for granted. In the hard work of the next few days, it can be said with certainty that Britain will advocate adopting the Lytton Report as much as possible, knowing that the only hope for peace is for China and Japan to approach each other based on the direction indicated in the Lytton Report. Therefore, the report of the Nineteenth Special Committee must be based on the Lytton Report, with attachments whose nature and impact are currently impossible to predict. (Reuters dispatch from Geneva, 21st)

Germany Declares Neutrality in the Sino-Japanese Dispute 9

New Ways to Resolve the Dispute Will Be Presented to the League of Nations

Communist Party Members Criticize the Government for Leaning Towards Japan

(Berlin) German Foreign Minister Neurath stated in the Foreign Affairs Committee of the Reichstag today that Germany will provide a plan to resolve the dispute over the Sino-Japanese Manchuria case at the League of Nations General Assembly. However, the details have not yet been released, only a solemn declaration that Germany will remain completely neutral. He believes the government already has a solution acceptable to all parties. According to reports, Communist Party members in the German Parliament have accused the current government of being pro-Japanese. (National Telegraph dispatch, 21st)

The Key to Resolving the Sino-Japanese Case Lies with Britain; Sir Lytton Publishes an Article 10

(London) "The Sunday Chronicle" published an article by Sir Lytton, chairman of the Manchurian Investigation Commission. First, he described the various elements of the Far East problem, and then explained the remedies, requesting the League of Nations to make a decision. But what is the possible method? Sir Lytton replied, "Any material action by the powers can be regarded by Japan as a reason for war. Only through spiritual pressure can Japan be made to follow the path of the League of Nations. If the powers in Geneva unanimously approve the League of Nations' resolution against Japan, Japan will sooner or later concede. In short, Britain should bear the greatest responsibility in future events. Whatever the League of Nations should decide, it should be decided. The eyes of the world are now focused on Britain. Britain should take the initiative, because Britain is Japan's former ally. If you want to make Japan approach the League of Nations, it should be guided by Britain. The difficulty of the responsibility borne by politicians in Geneva is probably no greater than that of Foreign Minister Simon." (Havas dispatch, 22nd)

The League of Nations Has Failed to Uphold Justice; Small Countries Are in Constant Danger; France's Attitude Differs from Britain's 11

According to a Nagoya Shimbun dispatch from Geneva on the 16th, representatives of small Nordic countries have fully understood the truth of the Manchurian problem and the behavior of the Japanese. Now the League's own resolution has created a bad precedent of favoring Japan. In the future, when dealing with European problems, it is difficult to guarantee that it will not follow suit and endanger the positions of the small countries. Therefore, they strongly advocate that Japan withdraw from the League and reduce the scope of the League of Nations to become a European alliance. On the other hand, Spanish representative Madariaga, although not attending the meeting, is still opposing Japan from the sidelines in the capacity of staff. French representatives Caudry and others, with the Radical Socialist Party as their background, represent the Pengu Cabinet and advocate upholding the dignity of the League of Nations, which is increasingly becoming unfavorable.

(Paris) The Socialist Party's newspaper "Le Populaire" commented on the Sino-Japanese incident that the proposal to be put forward by the League of Nations Committee of Nineteen after the failure of the mediation procedures should have the nature of satisfying world opinion, because Japan's military actions have indeed shocked world opinion. In order to satisfy world opinion, the League of Nations should give a serious judgment to the aggressor, because only in this way can world opinion rise up against Japan and economic and diplomatic sanctions can be implemented to stop Japan from annexing Manchuria and Jehol. The League of Nations has wasted precious time, and now it must act as soon as possible. (Havas dispatch, 22nd)

Britain's Pro-Japanese Attitude Remains Unchanged; Trade Will Be Affected; London Receives Report 12

(London) The Geneva correspondent of the London Observer reported that people in Geneva now have a very real impression that Britain's attitude towards Japan has become firmer in the past week. Many believe that friendly pressure from the United States may be related to this, but some also say that the reports from the Far East received by the British government have also had an impact. According to this report, the Chinese have expressed resentment at Britain's pro-Japanese attitude, and British trade with China will be affected. Furthermore, if Japan gains greater advantages on the Asian continent, British trade will also suffer. (Reuters dispatch, 22nd)

Japanese Government Instructs Matsuoka, the Representative 13

Instructing him not to rush to withdraw, lest he isolate himself.

He must continue to strive to implement his consistent claims.

(Tokyo) The Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs originally expected that the League of Nations' compromise with Japan would not be finalized until British Foreign Minister Simon returned to Geneva. Unexpectedly, the Committee of Nineteen Nations rejected Japan's modifications at the meeting on the 21st and decided to invoke Article 15, Paragraph 4 to forcibly mediate the Sino-Japanese dispute. The Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs was shocked when it heard the news and immediately held an emergency ministerial meeting. It will issue the following telegram to Plenipotentiary Matsuoka tonight or tomorrow morning: (1) The Japanese government sincerely hopes that the harmonious means of Article 15, Paragraph 3 can mediate the Sino-Japanese dispute. However, the Committee of Nineteen Nations is so anxious to end the dispute by invoking Article 15, Paragraph 4 that it cannot but consider its harmony a failure. The responsibility should be borne by the League of Nations itself. The delegation should take appropriate opportunities to declare that Japan is not responsible for this. (2) The Japanese government is not afraid to use Paragraph 4. The delegation does not need to take any further action to prevent the League of Nations from invoking the article. (3) There is no need to withdraw from the League of Nations because of the invocation of Paragraph 4, because member states have the right not to accept it. The Japanese government has decided that the delegation will remain in the League of Nations and observe its changes. However, the delegation must step up its efforts to implement Japan's claims. (United Press dispatch, 22nd)

Japanese Military Authorities Vehemently Call for Withdrawal from the League of Nations; Not Afraid Even If Paragraph 4 Is Invoked 14

(Tokyo) With the League of Nations poised to apply Article 15, Paragraph 4 of the Covenant, the Army authorities issued the following statement last night in the form of a talk: The point of contention between the League of Nations and Japan is that it does not consider the special circumstances of the Far East, but forcefully applies the principles applicable to disputes between modern countries. Small countries unrelated to the Far East are defending themselves, clinging to ideal arguments, and even expressing the attitude of hoping that Japan will withdraw. The situation of advocating the application of Article 15, Paragraph 4 is very strong. The Committee of Nineteen Nations abandoned its efforts to resolve the problem too early and hurriedly sought to end it, openly declaring the League of Nations' own weakness and failure to the world, which is a pity for the League of Nations. If the League of Nations persists to the end, Japan will withdraw without hesitation. Moreover, it does not care about applying Paragraph 4. After self-reflection and correction, I will go even if there are millions of people. It is impossible to predict what will happen after Paragraph 4 is applied. The League of Nations is asking for it itself and should be responsible for all situations arising from it. (Dentsu dispatch, 22nd)

Soviet Russia Refutes Japanese Rumors 15

(Moscow) The Soviet government gazette "Izvestia" published the following news today: "On January 15, the Japanese military department published a provocative report in various Japanese newspapers, fabricating rumors about the Soviet government and the future Soviet embassy in China. The report said, "The Third International recently proposed to the Chinese Communist Party to focus its attention on strengthening the Red Army and expressed that it would provide the greatest financial assistance from the Soviet embassy in China, which will be opened soon." It also falsely accused that the Soviet Union and the Chinese government have reached an agreement to develop trade relations between the two countries, the purpose of which is to exclude the goods of other countries from the Chinese market. Therefore, Soviet Ambassador to Japan Taranovsky visited Japanese Vice Foreign Minister Arita on the 19th, representing the Soviet government in protesting against the absurd anti-Soviet news issued by the Japanese military department in the gazette." (TASS dispatch, 21st)

Foreign Minister Luo Refutes Uchida's Absurd Remarks 16

Japan's Dream of Expanding Territory Is Far from Being Awakened

Declares That There Can Be No Talk of Compromise Until the Puppet State Is Abolished

(Nanjing) Regarding the diplomatic speech made by Japanese Foreign Minister Uchida on the 21st in the Japanese Parliament, Foreign Minister Luo Wengan issued the following statement today: "Foreign Minister Uchida's speech to the Japanese Parliament on the 21st, judging solely from its relationship to Japan's atrocities in the Eastern Provinces, is sufficient to prove that Japan's military aggression and dream of expanding territory are far from being awakened. Since Uchida's first speech on the Far Eastern situation last August, several months have passed, but Uchida has not diminished his public contempt for the authority of the League of Nations, the dignity of international treaties, and the effectiveness of international law. In this speech, Uchida again involved the puppet state of Manchukuo, not only acknowledging its existence as legitimate, but also going further to talk about its possibility of expansion, and publicly declaring Japan's determination to invade Jehol. Such absurd views and arguments, people do not want to waste their time refuting them, because the Chinese government and the League of Nations investigation team have already refuted them completely. What we want to solemnly declare is that China's attitude is very clear and firm, that the puppet state of Manchukuo created and supported by the Japanese must be abolished, and that China must restore its inherent sovereignty in the Eastern Provinces. Before the Japanese puppet organization is formally declared illegal and abolished, so-called mediation, reconciliation, or any other solution is impossible." (Central News Agency dispatch, 22nd)

US Media's Criticism of Japanese Foreign Minister's Speech Treating Treaties as Waste Paper 17

(Washington) Red Covenant Forum's commentary stated that Foreign Minister Uchida's speech was tantamount to declaring that international treaties are equal to waste paper and cannot prevent Japan's military desires. Japan's Monroe Doctrine clearly attempts to monopolize the Far East, creating Japan's special undertakings, emulating the United States' prohibition of non-Americans from interfering in American affairs. Furthermore, Japan rashly acts as a Far Eastern policeman, which is not enough to promote peace, but endangers the vested interests of other countries. The Washington Post editorial stated that the war debt issue must be discussed jointly with other important matters, such as the Far Eastern problem and the dignity of treaties. (Central News Agency dispatch, 22nd)

Duan Qirui Arrived in Beijing Yesterday from Ping; Chiang and Other Important Figures Welcomed Him in Person

Duan Talks About Anti-Japanese Opinions and Defending Against Insults 18

(Nanjing) Duan Qirui has been away from politics and living in Tianjin, eating vegetarian food and worshiping Buddha for many years. After the Yuguan Incident, the Japanese army's invasion of Jehol became more urgent, and rumors were spread to confuse the public. Duan, aware of the noise and evil environment, resolutely left Tianjin for Beijing on the 20th with Qian Xinzhi, the representative sent by Chairman Chiang to welcome him, and Wu Guangxin, the former Chief of the Army. He arrived in Pukou at 8:00 AM on the 22nd.

Welcoming Personnel 19

Chairman Chiang sent Zhu Peide, who was also acting as Director of Training, as a representative to welcome him. Other welcomers included Zhang Qun, He Yaozu, Huang Musong, Yang Jie, Xu Shiying, Yang Yongtai, Yao Zong, etc., who all gathered at the Xiaguan Ferry Terminal at 7:10 AM and took a ferry across the river to Pukou to welcome him. Members of the Anhui Association in Beijing brought white cloth banners with the words "Welcome Mr. Duan, the Creator of the Three Republics" and "Welcome Mr. Duan, the Veteran of Anti-Japanese and National Salvation." In total, there were about a hundred people who came to the station to welcome him.

State of Alert 20

This morning, the Xiaguan area, the Gendarmerie Headquarters, and the Capital Police Department were ordered to increase patrols and security. In addition to the Jilu Railway Police adding posts at Pukou Station and the Ferry Terminal, the Gendarmerie Headquarters and the Capital Police Department sent out gendarmerie police to take charge of security.

Duan Qirui Arrived in Beijing Yesterday

Arrival at the Station 21

Mr. Duan took two special sleeping cars prepared by the Jilu Railway, attached to car "202" heading south, using two locomotives to pull and push. He arrived at Pukou at 8:00 AM sharp. After Mr. Duan's car drove into the platform, the welcoming personnel successively boarded the car to pay their respects. Mr. Duan met them one by one in the carriage, nodding in greeting. Mr. Duan was dressed in a robe and mandarin jacket yesterday, with a fox fur coat and a black velvet square top hat. His spirit was slightly weak, but when he spoke, he was energetic. Although he needed support when walking, he was not hunchbacked. In addition to Qian Yongming and Wu Guangxin, those who accompanied Duan south this time included Wei Zonghan, the former commander of the Ninth Division, and Duan's nephew Hong, as well as a servant. There was a lot of luggage.

Taking the Ferry Across the River 22

After Mr. Duan met the welcoming personnel, Yao Zong immediately asked Mr. Duan to get out of the car and board the rattan sedan chair prepared on the platform, which was carried to the ferry terminal. The accompanying personnel and welcoming personnel also successively walked out of the platform and boarded the Chengping Ferry together. The ferry set sail across the river at 8:15 AM.

Conversation on the Ferry 23

On the ferry, Mr. Duan was introduced by Xu Shiying to talk to the welcoming personnel. He praised Chief Supervisor Zhu Peide and others quite a bit. Then he talked to Yang Jie, the commander of the Yangtze River Fortress, saying that when I (Duan referring to himself) was the Chief of the Army in the first year of the Republic, I advocated strengthening the construction of the Yangtze River Fortress so that it could become a weapon for national defense. Otherwise, the door would be wide open, and how could it not be taken advantage of by the violent enemy? His words seemed to be full of emotion. Later, he said that he did not want to be entertained by all parties during this trip south. In Beijing, he could stay at his sister's house at No. 19 Shenjia Lane, and then go to Shanghai. He was then informed that the Lishi Society had already prepared everything, and Mr. Duan agreed not to go to his sister's house, but to stay at the Lishi Society.

Chiang Welcomed Him in Person 24

The Chengping Ferry arrived at Xiaguan at 8:30 AM. Mr. Duan originally planned to go ashore immediately and enter the city, but at that time he received a call from the Military Affairs Committee, saying that Chairman Chiang had already arrived in his own car to welcome him. After hearing the news, Mr. Duan repeatedly said "No need" "No need", I can go to meet him. Chiang's car had arrived at the terminal, and he immediately abandoned the car and boarded the ferry to pay his respects, performing the ceremony of teacher and student, and frequently inquired about his health. Duan replied that his leg had been sick for years, making walking difficult. In recent months, his stomach had been sick and he had eaten little. It can be seen that he was old and weak. Fortunately, he had been feeling comfortable recently. After the greetings, Chiang immediately asked Duan to get off the ferry and board Chiang's own car, No. 318. Duan sat in the middle, and Chiang and Wu Guangxin sat on the left and right, and immediately sped towards the Lishi Society. The welcoming personnel and Mr. Duan's entourage also rushed to get on the bus and enter the city. The luggage was sent by the Lishi Society to be loaded into cars and transported to the Lishi Society residence.

Mr. Duan's Speech 25

After Mr. Duan's car arrived at the Lishi Society, he went upstairs and talked with Chairman Chiang for forty minutes. Then he met Ma Liang and others, and had some tea and snacks. Then he answered the questions asked by reporters in writing as follows: (Reporter asked) What are Mr. Duan's opinions on resisting Japan? (Mr. Duan replied) At this time of national crisis, the government already has a whole set of policies and methods for defending against insults. Regardless of whether it is in the government or in the opposition, we should all rise up to support it. Although Rui is old, he should also strive to follow the people of the country. (Asked) How does Mr. Duan feel about this trip south? (Answer) It has been more than ten years since I have been to Nanjing. What I have seen and heard here is completely (continues on page 6)

new. Everyone from Commander-in-Chief Chiang down is full of vigor, and I deeply admire them. However, passing through the residences along the way, I still feel that there is a phenomenon of dilapidation and disrepair. From this, it can be known the suffering of the villagers. Cultivating vitality still requires effort. (Asked) Can Mr. Duan tell us about his future whereabouts? (Answer) My sister is in Beijing and my youngest daughter lives in Shanghai. Chiang Hosted a Welcoming Dinner 26

Members of the Central Committee Zhang Qun, Yang Yongtai, Secretary-General of the Three Provinces Bandit Suppression Headquarters, Xiong Shihui, Chairman of the Jiangxi Provincial Government, and others, thinking that Mr. Duan had traveled a long way and was quite tired along the way, hosted a welcoming dinner for Mr. Duan at the Central Hotel at noon. At 7:00 PM, Chairman Chiang also hosted a banquet for Mr. Duan, Wu Guangxin, Wei Zonghan, and others at his private residence in the Military Academy, and invited various important figures to accompany him.

Worshipping at the Mausoleum This Morning 27

Mr. Duan believed that he was most familiar with the Premier in his life. However, since the Premier passed away in Ping and was buried in Jinling, he had not seen his remains. Now, when he is in Beijing, in order to admire the remains of the Premier, he set off on the 23rd to visit the mausoleum on Zijin Mountain and respectfully present a wreath. The Lishi Society notified the Premier's Mausoleum Management Committee yesterday to prepare everything. (Special dispatch, 22nd)

Duan Answers Jiang's Visit 28

At 11:00 AM, Duan Qirui traveled by car to the military academy to return the visit of Chairman Jiang, spoke for half an hour, and returned to the Lìzhì Society. In the afternoon at 5:00 PM, he led his entourage to Yìjiàqiáo to visit his younger sister, Madam Chen, and inquired about her recent situation. At 7:00 PM that evening, he attended a banquet hosted by Jiang. Yu Youren, Dai Chuanxian, Zhang Qun, Qian Xinzhi, Xu Shiying, and others were all invited to accompany him. Duan is scheduled to go to Shanghai by train on the evening of the 23rd. Duan's nephew, Hong Tan, said that Duan has been living in Tianjin in seclusion for almost ten years, not asking about worldly affairs. Since the September 18th Incident, the Japanese have repeatedly spread rumors in an attempt to discredit him. In fact, although Duan is old, his nationalistic thinking is very strong, so how could he resort to such a poor strategy? The people of the country should remain calm and unite to resist foreign aggression, and not be misled by these rumors. Duan has no specific plans for the major strategy of resisting Japan. If the government seeks his advice, he will provide references based on his experiences. He does not plan to stay in Beijing for long and plans to go to Shanghai on the evening of the 23rd. Jiang has already sent Qian Xinzhi to Shanghai to find a residence for him. In Shanghai, he plans to stay for a week or so, and then go to Putuo Temple in Hangzhou for a tour, enjoying the spring scenery of the Jiangnan region. The date of his return north has not yet been determined. (Special dispatch of the 22nd)

Japan Plans to Change its Invasion of Rehe Plan

Military Seemingly to Emphasize Lingyuan, Jiumenkou, and Other Places, Enemy Heavy Troops Gathered Between Suizhong, Xingcheng, and Yuguan 29

Lingyuan is Already Critical, Garrison Troops are Strictly Defending, Zheng Guilin Leads Troops to Cut off the Enemy's Rear

Kailu's Feng Zhanhai and Li Haiqing's Troops Repulse the Japanese 6th Division 30

(Beiping) The Japanese army, seeing that our defense in Chaoyang and Kailu is very strict, combined with high mountains and steep ridges, rendering tanks and armored vehicles ineffective, is preparing to change its strategy. The Japanese 8th Division stationed at Yaowangmiao in Lingnan and a part of the Mogi Cavalry Brigade attacking Yu County will attack Lingyuan from Lingnan. These are all main roads. Currently, the Japanese are advancing through surveying and mapping from Lingnan County. In the main road gully of the first district of Lingnan, more than 500 Japanese cavalry and infantry of the 8th Division have been discovered, along with military supplies and four tanks. Zheng Guilin, the Righteous Army of Lingyuan County, upon hearing the news, led his troops to cut off the enemy's rear route. Our garrison, the 254th Brigade of Lingyuan County, has already taken strict precautions. Rumors are rampant in Lingyuan. County Magistrate Zhang Danchi held a meeting with local groups to discuss resistance measures. On the 21st, a Japanese aircraft from the Jinzhou Aircraft Factory flew to Lingyuan County for reconnaissance. When passing the Lingyuan County Government, it mistook our Public Security Bureau and the Public Security Cavalry Unit as military garrisons and scattered a large number of red and green paper leaflets. It flew east for about fifteen minutes without dropping bombs. (Special dispatch of the 22nd)

(Beiping) The enemy has repeatedly provoked our Nanling positions with artillery fire, but has been repulsed by our troops. Seeing that our Kailu and Nanling area's positions are solid and difficult to capture, the military invasion of Rehe seems to be focusing on Lingyuan and Jiumenkou in Jinxi. Therefore, the enemy's heavy troops are concentrated between Suizhong, Xingcheng, and Yuguan. Yesterday, the enemy's Mogi Cavalry Unit, about 1,200 men, and 500 infantrymen, carrying four tanks and eight field guns, moved from the Lingyuan Avenue outside Jiumenkou towards the Rehe border of Lingyuan. They have already made contact with Zheng Guilin's outposts in the main road gully of Shanzuizi. Our Righteous Army is currently uniting with the militia in the Chapeng area to fight back. (Special dispatch of the 22nd)

(Beiping) Our troops have built several defensive lines in a certain area west of the Shi River. Defenses have also been set up near Shimen Village and the Liujiang River. Jiumenkou is still guarded by a certain brigade. Defenses are very strict along the avenue from Jiumenkou to Pingquan. Outside Jiumenkou, the number of puppet troops has increased to more than 3,000. Zhang Jinghui, the commander-in-chief of the puppet army, arrived in Jinzhou from Changchun a few days ago to inspect and discuss the military invasion of Rehe with Yoshiichi Nishi, the commander of the Japanese 8th Division. A part of the Suzuki Brigade has been withdrawn from Yuguan City to Jinzhou, and the 4th Regiment has been transferred to fill the defense. More than a dozen artillery emplacements have been built at the west gate of Yuguan. Three trains of armored vehicles are parked at the station. Police of the puppet state patrol inside and outside Yuguan City. Japanese and Manchukuo flags are hung at the station. Refugees fleeing Yuguan City are not allowed to go west. The Japanese army has dispatched more than 20 sentries along the South China Sea. The fare for rickshaws from Yuguan to Qinhuangdao is about fifteen yuan. Two Japanese torpedo boats and one flagship are stationed on the sea off Qinhuangdao. (Special dispatch of the 22nd)

Zhang Jinghui Arrives in Suizhong to Command 31

(Beiping) Traitor Zhang Jinghui arrived in Suizhong today, planning a large-scale invasion of Rehe. Puppet troops are moving towards the Rehe border one after another. This morning, three more trains of Japanese troops were added near Chaoyang Temple. The Feng Zhanhai and Li Haiqing units of Kailu repulsed the Japanese 6th Division in the Senlütu area, killing more than 40 Japanese soldiers. Japanese troops in Kailu, disguised as Chinese, purchased a large amount of grain, which has been transported to the Tongliao area. (Special dispatch of the 22nd)

(Beiping) The puppet state army under Cheng Guorui has three regiments stationed in Yixian, each with 200-300 men. Guns and horses are provided by the recruits themselves. Cheng himself recruited more than 5,000 soldiers in Jinxi County and issued them guns, ammunition, and clothing in preparation for invading Rehe. Five to six hundred Japanese soldiers and one tank are stationed in Yixian. Japanese troops are building fortifications in the Jiaoshan Temple, Yuxi Matouzhuang, and southern coast areas. (Special dispatch of the 22nd)

Japanese Troops in Yuguan Complete Preparations 32

(Beiping) Enemy ships shone searchlights along the coast of Qinhuangdao all night. Qinhuangdao is peaceful. The Japanese troops in Yuguan have completed their preparations. Three trains of armored vehicles are parked at the station. The locomotive appears ready to move west. Merchants in Yuguan report that the Japanese and puppet troops will launch a general offensive against our army at the end of the lunar year. Enemy aircraft have been conducting reconnaissance flights over Haiyang and Qinhuangdao for days, but have not dropped bombs. Shimen Village has been in a state of ceasefire for days. About 400 enemy Mogi cavalrymen have been dispatched to Hei Shantou for reinforcement. Outside Jiumenkou, the Righteous Army is engaged in fierce fighting with enemy cavalry in Huangtuling and Yongan Fort. (Special dispatch of the 22nd)

(Beiping) Yesterday, in Qinhuangdao, more than 300 Japanese cavalry, three or four tanks, and twelve cars invaded our line of defense at Lishugoumen. They were repulsed by our garrison troops. (Special dispatch of the 22nd)

Enemy Reinforcements Again Increase at Jiumenkou 33

Linyu On the 22nd, enemy reinforcements of more than 700 men arrived at Jiumenkou. At dusk on the 21st, four of our army's scouts clashed with enemy sentries in Hujiazhuang on the east bank of the Shi River. The enemy fired more than a dozen shells and called in one tank, two machine guns, and more than 20 infantrymen from the city to surround our scouts. Our soldiers fought bravely, killing several enemy soldiers. One of our soldiers was killed or wounded, and the rest retreated gradually. (Special dispatch of the 22nd)

The puppet state army dispatched from Suizhong has advanced to the vicinity of Shamao Mountain. (Beiping) A few days ago, four Japanese aircraft came to Heicun, 100 li from Beipiao, and dropped dozens of bombs, all of which landed in the riverbed and forest. (Special dispatch of the 22nd)

Northeastern Japanese Army Will Fully Open to Rehe 35

(Beiping) The Northeastern Japanese Army will fully reinforce the Rehe border. Only one regiment of Japanese soldiers and about 300 puppet troops are currently stationed in the Yuguan area. Because Rehe is not easy to advance, the Japanese army decided to transfer the 1st Division to reinforce the Northeast. The 49th Infantry Regiment and the 7th Field Heavy Artillery Regiment of that division had already crossed the Yalu River to Andong on the 19th and immediately took the Anshen Railway to transfer to the puppet Fengshan Railway to Kaiyuguan to increase defense. (Special dispatch of the 22nd)

The Front of Shi River Has Been Peaceful for Days 36

(Beiping) The front of the Shi River has been peaceful for days. The enemy is forcibly conscripting laborers in various places near Yuguan to dig trenches and is covering the entire southern coast with barbed wire and electric fences. The enemy seems to be adopting a defensive posture. (Special dispatch of the 22nd)

Japanese Armored Vehicles Open Fire on Nanling 37

(Beiping) Japanese armored vehicles opened fire on Nanling last night, making contact with our army guarding Nanling. The defenses in Chaoyang, Lingyuan, and Pingquan are extremely solid. (Special dispatch of the 22nd)

(Beiping) Japanese troops in Chaoyang and Nanling are rushing to build defensive works and are forcibly conscripting carts. Residents have all fled. Nanling is only 120 li from Chaoyang County, and is surrounded by high mountains. The Japanese army has repeatedly used over-mountain artillery to fire, causing no losses. Only the houses of the residents along the mountain have been destroyed. Chaoyang is currently extremely cold. There are more than 30,000 troops and puppet police stationed along Chaoyang. More than 300 Japanese troops drove in from Suizhong but did not disembark. Three trains of armored vehicles are stationed in Chaoyang Temple, and two are stationed in Nanling. There has been no artillery fire in recent days. Chaoyang County has suffered from war, drought, and banditry this year, and the local area is extremely impoverished. (Special dispatch of the 22nd)

Rehe Anti-Japanese Army Would Rather Be Shattered Like Jade 38

(Beiping) The 6th Route Commander of the Rehe Anti-Japanese Army, Yan Bowei, cut off the railway between Xingcheng and Baimiao at dawn on the 20th and fought fiercely with the Japanese army guarding the railway. Both sides suffered heavy casualties. Yan et al. sent a telegram to Beiping, planning to join forces with friendly armies in Jinzhou within a short period of time to recover the lost territory. They would rather be shattered like jade than survive as a whole. (Special dispatch of the 22nd)

(Beiping) The Rehe Righteous Army under Huang Shouchu, with more than 5,000 men, is stationed in Jingpeng and Linxi counties, planning to go to southern Rehe to assist Tang in resisting Japan within a few days. (Special dispatch of the 22nd)

Tang Jwu's Troops are Stationed in the Rehe Border Area 39

Rehe The troops of Tang Juwu, the commander-in-chief of the 3rd Army of the Volunteer Army, are stationed in various places in the Rehe border area. Tang himself arrived in Chengde on the 21st, planning to carry arms and military supplies on the morning of the 23rd to go to the front to prepare to kill the enemy. (Special dispatch of the 22nd)

Wu Peifu Talks About the Current Situation 40

If the people of the country can fully realize this and concentrate their strength to resist Japan, there will definitely be a considerable chance of success in the future. He hopes that the people of the country will automatically unite to resist Japan. He previously received telegrams from various groups in the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce saying what they would do, but he only smiled at them. Mr. Zhichuan's entry into Beijing this time has opened a bright path for the current situation. The Beijing authorities have repeatedly sent special envoys here, hoping that he would go to Beijing, but he has no intention of going to Beijing for the time being. If he suddenly goes south, rumors will inevitably arise. It is shameful for foreigners that many wealthy families in Beiping and Tianjin have moved. If everyone can use the money spent on moving to disaster relief, more lives will be saved. He will not lag behind in resisting Japan, but he does not want to express his opinions on politics. (Special dispatch of the 22nd)

Puyi is Only a Three-Layer Slave in Changchun 41

(Beiping) News came out from the Prince Gong's Mansion that Puwei, who is 54 years old, has recently been handling his wife's funeral in Lushun. He has a bad relationship with Puyi and rarely interacts with him. Puyi gifted Wei 500 yuan for funeral expenses. Puwei is the firstborn son, and has two younger brothers, Punuo and Puhui, who are both born of concubines and have been involved in litigation with Puwei. Puyi is a three-layer slave in Changchun. He must abide by Zheng Xiaoxu in everything, Zheng abides by Komai, and Komai obeys the Kwantung Army. Zheng hands over all official matters to Pu for signature. When Pu wants to see them, Zheng scolds him, saying, "Just sign, what's there to see?" Pu often sheds tears when no one is around. (Special dispatch of the 22nd)

Current Commentary

Today's Two Major Problems 43

Today, there are two major problems obstructing our view. One is "resisting Japan," and the other is "stabilizing the lives of the masses." Stabilizing the lives of the masses is "pacifying the interior," while resisting Japan is "repelling foreign aggression."

What does it mean to say that those who talk about saving the country today all say that saving the country should start with "pacifying the interior?" However, how can the interior be pacified? It cannot be done with force, nor can it be done with small favors. The only way is to stop the source of the chaos. Where does the chaos come from? From hunger and cold. Xunzi did not say, "Only when clothing and food are sufficient do people know honor and disgrace." When people have no food to eat and no clothes to wear, the old and weak wander, and the young and strong are displaced. If they fill the wilderness with starvation, and are driven by the necessities of life, how can the people not be in chaos? The world has no people who like chaos, only the masses who take risks. When driven by the necessities of life, a single person calls out at night, and responses arise from all around. Examining historical records, they are full of examples. The people already do not know where they will die. If they are threatened with force and fear of death, how is this different from pouring soup to stop boiling? If the source of the chaos is not stopped, how can the chaos be quelled? Therefore, the only way for us to talk about pacifying the interior today is to "stabilize the lives of the people," so that everyone has food to eat and clothes to wear. In good years, they are well-fed and warm, and in bad years, they will not be displaced. The people know the joy of living and will naturally not be willing to take risks to make decisions. If not, officials are well-fed and comfortable, while the people are both cold and hungry, compounded by natural and man-made disasters, and extorted by arbitrary levies and taxes. The people have nowhere to cry out. As last winter, there were 4,000 disaster victims in Henan who fled to Tianjin to escape death. They were not allowed to enter and were sent south. The south also telegraphed a refusal. They wandered along the roads, and the officials turned a blind eye and pushed the responsibility on each other. Then what value do the people place on having a country? Therefore, today, talking about stabilizing the lives of the people is naturally the responsibility of the government, and there is no room for shirking or delaying.

What does it mean to say "resisting Japan?" Since September 18th, Japan has wanted to strangle our throats every day and seize our lives with one move. Its continental policy has been thought out carefully and thoroughly. For a year, Japan's atrocities against us have only increased and have never stopped. This is by no means accidental. Even the silence and observation of the great powers, who are unwilling to make righteous statements, each has its own political and economic background, and there is a reason for this. Our policy of non-resistance cannot stop the invaders from moving forward, nor can appeals to the world and complaints win us fair assistance. Then what else can we expect and what else can we hope for today other than to seek self-defense and self-salvation through our own efforts? What is the way to self-defense and self-salvation? It is resistance. It is struggle. With the greatest determination, we can fight with all our might and eventually achieve the final victory. Otherwise, we will be timid and seek temporary peace, neither fighting nor making peace, and be slaughtered by others. In fact, we are just waiting for death.

The people are suffering deeply today. However, we dare to say that their suffering is for the sake of protecting the survival of our nation and for resisting the aggression of the violent. Then, no matter how much suffering there is, our people will have no complaints. This is for the masses to seek the last way out. There is no way to get it without suffering. If the suffering is not for resisting violence, but merely consumes the spirit and wealth of saving the country in the dark and invisible, then foreign troubles and internal worries will oppress each other. The future of our country will be in great difficulty. We really do not know how it will end.

Therefore, in terms of the current situation, "resisting Japan" and "stabilizing the lives of the people" are both the most urgent and serious problems at present. But weighing the urgency and importance, we believe that "resisting Japan" is even more urgent than "stabilizing the lives of the people."

National Army Begins Large-Scale Encirclement and Suppression of Jiangxi Bandits

Various Arrangements Completed, Bandit Retreat Routes Cut Off, No Bandit Traces in the Fuzhou Area Below Huwan 44

(Nanchang) The National Army did not want to startle the grass and scare away the snake with regards to the pseudo-1st, 3rd, and 5th Army Corps, and planned to have the Fujian 19th Route Army and the Southwestern garrison troops cut off the bandit retreat routes. The Fuzhou side then launched an attack. Currently, the Chen Cheng and Wu Qiwu armies, as well as Sun Lianzhong, Zhou Zhizhiu, Luo Zhuoying, Zhou Hunyuan, Li Yunjie, and Xu Kexiang, have completed their arrangements. The Li Mo'an division has also arrived in Fuzhou. Liu Zhennian and Liu Kan will also arrive. A large-scale encirclement and suppression will begin. (Special dispatch of the 21st)

(Nanchang) Military News: Zhao Bosheng, the commander-in-chief of the pseudo-5th Army Corps, was killed in action in various battles at Huangshidu, and 3,000 bandits were eliminated. The pseudo-central government changed Ningdu to Bosheng County in memory of the bandit Zhao. Because the retreat route of each bandit was cut off by the 19th Route Army, they retreated from Liufang and Xuwan. We are following closely. Sun's division and Feng's brigade are advancing towards Chongren's pseudo-5th division. The county seat can be recovered soon. (Special dispatch of the 21st)

(Nanchang) Jiang is scheduled to arrive on the 23rd. The various welcoming Jiang meetings stipulated that 7 welcoming arches would be set up by various groups. When Jiang arrives, the entire city will fly county flags, and citizens will stand on both sides of the road to welcome him respectfully. Xiong Shihui and Fan Zhengbo will go to Xunyang to welcome him. (Special dispatch of the 22nd)

(Nanchang) Liu Kan's division came to the province from Xunyang today. Liu Zhennian has arrived in eastern Zhejiang. Li's division arrived in Fuzhou from the province yesterday. Morale is greatly boosted. The bandits attacking Fuzhou are in full retreat. The pseudo-1st Army Corps retreated to Fangping, the bandits in Dongxiang retreated to Lixu, and the pseudo-3rd Army Corps abandoned most of their supplies because they did not have time to move them. There are no traces of bandits in the Fuzhou area below Xuwan. The 19th Route Army entered Lichuan. Our Luo, Zhou, Sun, Wu, and Li divisions are advancing north along the Fuzhou River, adopting a pincer-like formation. After Jiang arrives, they will launch a general offensive under unified command. It is reported that Jiang sent a long telegram to the province yesterday, ordering all departments to concentrate on time. (Special dispatch of the 22nd)

(Nanjing) The Provincial Party Department and the Provincial Government established the Post-Suppression of Bandits Association on the 21st, which will: 1. Guide the masses to assist in the suppression of bandits; 2. Conduct propaganda; 3. Promote rural cooperation; 4. Build roads; 5. Recruit refugees; 6. Assist the army in clearing out the remaining bandits; 7. Organize mass self-defense groups; and 8. Requisition post-war personnel from various agencies. (Special dispatch of the 22nd)

Liaoxi Righteous Army Suddenly Attacks Zhangwu 45

Demolishes a Section of the Datong Railway Line and Engages in Fierce Fighting with the Enemy for Four Hours Before Retreating

(Beiping) The Liaoxi Righteous Army, led by Wang Xianting, has been lurking in the mountains around Tai'an and Heishan. On the 17th, Wang led more than 3,000 men to launch a sudden attack on the Taimen of Zhangwu, and demolished a section of the Datong Railway and the Xinlitun Railway to the north. They engaged in fierce fighting with the Japanese and puppet troops in the area for four hours before retreating southwest. They are currently stationed in a certain area and will contact Feng Zhanhai and other units to continue their advance. (Special dispatch of the 22nd)

(Beiping) The Liaoning Righteous Army Commander, Tian Xiahao, appealed for assistance and will return to defense within days. His troops are concentrated in Tongliao awaiting orders. The Women's Red Cross Society has set up a rescue class, with 40 students in the class. After two weeks of training, they will be sent to the rear hospital to serve. (Special dispatch of the 22nd)

Japanese Merchants Raise Funds to Establish Bank in Northeast 46

(Harbin) The Chinese newspaper Dai said that a group of Japanese and "Manchu" merchants has been approved by the "Manchukuo" to raise funds to establish a bank with a limited liability company. The bank will have a fixed capital of 10 million Japanese yen and will specialize in developing the industrial and commercial industries of "Manchukuo" and provide loans to small businesses. It is reported that many merchants in Harbin, Changchun, and Shenyang, as well as the Yokohama Specie Bank and the South Manchuria Railway Company, have expressed their willingness to be shareholders of the bank. (Reuters dispatch of the 22nd)

Large Numbers of Submarines are Stationed in Vladivostok

Japanese Population Statistics: Over 90,390,000 87

Tokyo, 22nd (Japan United Press) - The Cabinet Statistics Bureau recently released an overview of the national census conducted in Showa 5 (1930), as follows: The confirmed population of Japan is 90,396,043, divided as follows: 64,450,005 in the mainland, 21,058,305 in Korea, 4,592,537 in Taiwan, and 295,198 in Karafuto (South Sakhalin).

Among the prefectures nationwide, Tokyo has the largest population, with 5,408,000 people, followed by Osaka with 3,540,000. Other areas with a population of over 2 million include Hokkaido, Hyogo, Aichi, and Fukuoka. The prefecture with the smallest population is Tottori, with 489,000 people. All others have more than 500,000. The number of men nationwide is 32,390,155, and the number of women is 32,059,850, meaning there are 330,000 more men than women. The number of unmarried people is 33,999,730, the number of married people is 15,210,480, the number of widowed people is 4,251,150, and the number of divorced people is 605,690. Of the widowed, men account for 1,080,000 and women for 3,600,000. There are three times as many widows as widowers.

US Prepares Negotiating Basis for War Debts; World Economic Issues Included in Agenda 90

Washington, 21st (National News Agency) - According to a report from London, some people in the British government believe that the United States will insist that Britain restore the gold standard before negotiating war debts. Upon hearing this, a statement was issued here stating that the United States has never mentioned the restoration of the gold standard. Yesterday's meeting between the two presidents and their advisors discussed Britain's request to open negotiations on war debts. Since Britain had already paid the war debt due in December, it was decided to grant their request. The rumor that the United States would insist on restoring the gold standard seems to have originated from the report of the experts preparing for the Geneva World Economic Conference, which suggested that countries should restore the gold standard. The US representative, William, participated in drafting the report and advocated for European countries to restore the gold standard. However, William did not insist that the recommendation to restore the gold standard be included in the report. The US State Department also stated today that it was acting on its own initiative and did not have instructions from the government. US officials are currently not commenting on William's proposal and have not publicly expressed support. As for the war debt issue, given the current situation, negotiations will proceed regardless of whether Britain restores the gold standard or not.

Currently, within the United States, since the President-elect Roosevelt expressed his approval yesterday for Secretary of State Stimson to prepare for the war debt conference, a good impression has been formed among senators and representatives. The conference agenda will have no restrictions, so he deeply appreciates Roosevelt's wise decision. However, Republican Senator Robinson still expressed his disapproval, saying that this move is a prelude to canceling or reducing war debts. He still supports the reservations stated by the Senate when former President Hoover proposed a one-year moratorium, and does not allow any further changes to the war debt solution.

Currently, experts from the State Department and Treasury Department have begun preparing a negotiating basis and will work closely with Democrat Moley and Roosevelt's other advisors. It is also reported that the two governments will agree on a procedure through existing diplomatic channels so that representatives of both countries can be certain of the proposals to be discussed before the meeting in February.

Policy of the New German Chancellor Schleicher (Berlin Correspondence)

Repealing Three Ordinances of the Previous Cabinet; Easing Antipathy Among Various Parties 93

The Papen Cabinet was a cabinet of the President, with no parliamentarians among its members. At the same time, it was also a disguised fascist cabinet. However, Papen himself was not a member of Hitler's National Socialist Party. What was his relationship with the Hitler Party? Originally, when Papen formed his cabinet, it was only in name, and the actual Prime Minister was Hitler. Therefore, although Prime Minister Papen was known for his cunning plots, he was actually a puppet Prime Minister. So what was the relationship between the Papen government and the Hitler Party? Broadly speaking, the Papen cabinet was under Hitler's guidance. In terms of power relations, General Schleicher, the Minister of Defense in the Papen cabinet, held the real power of the national defense forces and could command everything politically. In terms of the social foundation of this political relationship, the National Socialist Party was formed by the large landowners, heavy industrial capitalists, and military forces of Prussia.

German fascists (National Socialist Party) differ from Italian fascists. The Italian fascist regime was from the bottom up. After the March on Rome, they gained power. Germany is different. The National Socialist Party led by Hitler never marched on Berlin (although there are small conflicts in the streets every day, these conflicts are just brawls and do not count as political bloodshed). And the organization of the National Socialist Party is from top to bottom (the emerging capitalist forces in Germany are not very strong, and the organization of the proletariat and laborers from the Social Democratic Party to the Communist Party is very powerful). Therefore, the National Socialist Party has large landowners, financial capital, heavy industrial capitalists, and soldiers as its core, and the middle class with white-collar workers as the masses. Before the election on July 30th of this year, the National Socialist Party can be considered at its peak. The future of Germany was almost entirely in Hitler's hands. However, after the election, he did not get more than half of the seats. He had no possibility of dominating the political situation of the German Federation. So the Hitler Party was like the afternoon sun, and can only gradually decline from now on. Even if it still has some life, it can no longer have greater development. This is because of social power relations. Even if the parliament is dissolved several times and the elections are repeated several times, there will be no special changes. So the result of the general election on November 6th was that although Hitler still led the first party, he lost 35 seats. After the defeat of the Papen-Schleicher faction, political power became even more unstable. After December 3rd, the crown of Prime Minister of the German Federal Cabinet fell to General Schleicher. Needless to say, this is even more of a President's cabinet, and it is a purely military cabinet.

When Prime Minister Schleicher took office, he immediately issued a presidential order to repeal three articles of the "Law for the Protection of the Republic" promulgated by the former Papen cabinet, namely: 1. Abolishing the provision for special trials for political prisoners; 2. Abolishing the law requiring mandatory publication of government official statements; 3. Although the protection of the Republican system still exists, the ban on the return of former German Emperor Wilhelm II to Germany was removed. Whether the former Emperor will return to the country without any scruples is still a question. However, this is a major issue in Europe that is worth noting. First, why did the current government specifically order the lifting of the ban on the Kaiser's return to the country? Second, Germany is now in chaos and weak, and is about to reach the end of its rope. Is it necessary to use restoration to stir up people's hearts? The analysis of the first question is of course very subtle, and there will inevitably be many superficial observations. It is generally believed that the current President Hindenburg is a marshal, and Schleicher is also a general. The movement of German politics is accompanied by the sound of sabers. This is the rise of militarism, so it is inferred that it will lead to the restoration of the imperial system. In fact, things are not so simple. The current German soldiers cannot be completely represented by Marshal Hindenburg, who came from East Prussia. The officers in southern Germany are relatively liberal-minded. For example, former Minister of Defense General Groener was the initiator of advocating the abdication of the Emperor. The current Prime Minister General Schleicher also came from a poor peasant family. They do not necessarily have a conspiracy to restore the imperial system. The second question is no different from the deduction of the first question, but as far as the National Socialist Party is concerned, it is also very different from the National People's Party, which represents the remains of the landlords and nobles east of the Elbe River. They want to change the Lesser Germany ideology into the Greater Germany ideology. They have the spirit of the Holy Roman Empire, so although they show some goodwill to the former Emperor, they do not advocate restoration. Moreover, on the one hand, there is the Communist Party in the middle, and on the other hand, the Kaiser has already expressed his unwillingness to return to the country. Therefore, the main reason why the Schleicher cabinet abolished the ban on the Kaiser's return to the country is just a tactic to ease the antipathy of the National Socialist Party, the National People's Party, and the right-wing parties. (Berlin, December 18, 1932)

The Great Conspiracy of Japan to Disturb North China 94
