Xu Detang, Suspect in Kidnapping Case, Found Not Guilty 172

The Zhang family, whose daughter was kidnapped by bandits on the night of September 28th, 1928, at the entrance of No. 1928 Tongfu Road, later paid a ransom for her release. Subsequently, the police arrested a bandit named Li Zhangfu, who was sent to the First Special Court and sentenced to life imprisonment. Now, Li suddenly confessed that a person named Jin Jilin was also an accomplice. Zhao Fuhai, Cui Chengke, and Bao Tan Ma Derong, detectives from the Xinzha Police Station, investigated and found that Jin Jilin was actually Xu Detang (also known as Little Suzhou). They arrested Xu on the 22nd of last month at No. 14 Yile Lane, Fuxu Road, and sent him to the First Special Court. Li Zhangfu pointed out that Xu Detang was an alias of Jin Jilin and that he had met Xu twice in the bandit's hideout. However, Xu completely denied this, saying that the detective who arrested Li Zhangfu was Liang Chengyu, the No. 2 Chinese detective who is now a convicted criminal. Liang framed him to settle an old score because he did not know Li's whereabouts and Xu had led the arrest. The court was welcome to call Liang as a witness. He also hired lawyer Ye Fikang to defend him. Subsequently, the court ordered Liang to be brought in. Liang testified that it was indeed Xu who had led the arrest, and Xu was present when Li was arrested. Li did not say that Xu was an accomplice; otherwise, the police would have detained him. Judge Wu Tingqi verified the testimony and declared Xu Detang not guilty. The police lawyer, Wang Yaotang, requested that Xu be remanded in custody during the appeal period, which the court granted.

Searching Passengers and Seizing Money 173

丨Illegal Acts of Police Detectives丨

The Shanghai-Hangzhou railway stations have detectives search passengers. Originally, the Second District Police Station sent Gao to be stationed at the Shanghai station to execute. Later, the Public Security Bureau, considering the search matters to be important, added a supervisor to oversee. However, recently, the Investigation Team has also sent detectives to be stationed at the station for independent searches. The other day, a detective named Liu Shaoqing, along with his partner Du Jinlou, searched a passenger named Pan Shourong, suspected of carrying opium. Du Jinlou took advantage of the situation to seize thirty yuan of Pan's money, hiding it in his trouser leg. Pan Shourong discovered this, seized him and handed him over. Liu Shaoqing found the banknotes on his partner. When the station police chief arrived, he took both detectives to the Gaochang Temple Police Station. The patrolmen then submitted a report to the Second District, requesting that it be forwarded to the Public Security Bureau for disciplinary action, and handed over the two detectives. District Chief Jin Tian then submitted the case to the Bureau. After investigation by the Third Section, Du Jinlou was identified as impersonating a detective and was ordered to be sent to the Local Court for prosecution according to the law.

Jianghai Customs Recruiting Patrol Boat Drivers 175

丨Application Deadline: February 28th丨

The Marine Affairs Department of the Shanghai Customs is seeking patrol boat drivers due to the increasing complexity of maritime inspection duties and the inadequacy of the current number of drivers. Yesterday, it issued separate notices. Any citizen of the Republic of China under the age of 26, in good health, with excellent eyesight, knowledge of navigation and seamanship, proficiency in both Chinese and English, and with at least one year of experience as a watch officer on ships of 500 tons or more, holding a license from the Ministry of Transportation, may apply for the examination at the Marine Affairs Department office on the fifth floor of the Customs before February 28th. The Customs has scheduled the preliminary examination for March 13th, and the re-examination for March 14th, 15th, 16th, and 17th. Those who fail the preliminary examination will not be allowed to participate in the re-examination.

Reader's Advisor

Life and Hard Labor 176

丨Letter from Mr. Wu Qianxing丨

I am from Jinxi, Jiangxi. In October of this year, my home was occupied by the Red Army. I had no choice but to escape and seek a livelihood elsewhere. I originally planned to go to my cousin's place in Jinshi, Hunan, to find a position, but after arriving in Jinshi, I searched everywhere without success. My travel expenses were also exhausted. Being a stranger in a strange land, with no relatives or friends to turn to, I had to pawn all my belongings and become a peddler with a carrying pole. Unexpectedly, after less than three days, some idle thugs stole all my coppers and my carrying baskets in the evening, leaving me with no way up or down! My fate is so unfortunate; who could be worse off than me? Now, as a temporary measure, I want to help others as a hired hand, but no one will introduce me; I want to do hard labor, but I lack the strength to even bind a chicken, and my eyesight is not good. I want to beg from door to door, but I fear being met with scorn. A young man like me is reluctant to resort to such a last resort. Therefore, I am writing to you, hoping you can quickly provide guidance for my lost path. I would be extremely grateful!

Reply: After reading your letter, I cannot help but sigh! Speaking of which, your personal problem is very simple. Just get everyone to pool a few dozen dollars to give you a small business; or recommend a job for you, and it will be over. But your life is only a reflection of one drop in the ocean of the current decline of Chinese society; solving your personal problem, however, cannot solve the social problem that produced your life, the so-called "When shall I see a mansion of a million rooms, sheltering all the impoverished scholars of the world, and making them rejoice?" Not only is it impossible to do so, even if it is done, it is only a "treat the head when it hurts, treat the foot when it hurts" approach. Moreover, the duty of a newspaper, narrowed down, that is, the duty of the "Reader's Advisor" reporter, lies only in: (1) Pointing out the reader's difficulties in personal life problems: (2) Providing theoretical opinions on social problems: (3) From the standpoint of the greatest number of people, link the solution of the reader's personal life problems with the solution of the entire social life problem, and do not only see the trees and not see the forest. However, you still have a way to live, which is "doing hard labor". From your letter, you only said that you "lack the strength to even bind a chicken" and that your "eyesight is not good," and you did not say that there is no hard labor to do. The so-called hard labor is also of different levels. Some hard labor is naturally not suitable for people with weak physical strength, while others do not require much strength. If you have hard labor to do, then do hard labor. Because you have reached the end of the road, if you don't do hard labor, you can only die; that's right, there is another way: to be a thief; but being a thief can lead to imprisonment, or even execution, which also results in death. Between two evils, choose the lesser one. Doing hard labor can still save your life. You are young, and although the future of society seems dark, it has already revealed some light. Everyone is working hard to move forward, and one day it will completely become a society of hard labor, and then hard labor will be happy labor.

Re-answering Mr. Wang Xiping on the "Law of Panic Cycle" Problem 177

I have two points in response to Mr. Wang's letter published in this column on the 21st of this month. First, I said that Mr. Wang's wording was quite unclear because the editor and I mentioned that that passage was not easy to understand. After reading it, I felt that Mr. Wang's original text was indeed written a bit hastily, and some of the characters were not easy to recognize clearly. At the same time, the wording in it, such as "The statistics of import and export are realized, that is, the accumulation of production capital and commodity capital has a standard", is indeed somewhat difficult to understand. I strongly advocate that the wording published in newspapers be simple and easy to understand, so that the general readers can understand it, so I advocate asking Mr. Wang to organize it. Second, the tools of economics are already sufficient. The responsibility of us later students is to choose appropriate theoretical tools and apply them to the current facts. I am determined not to be as bold as the old Mr. Xu Qingfu in doing revolutionary and inventive work in economics. What is hateful right now are the bourgeois economists, that is, the current orthodox school, still deceiving themselves with outdated theories. So I feel that some correct theories should be instilled into the general readers. Everything I said in my writing is just applying existing tools to explain the facts at hand, and there is no newly invented theory. Speaking of the law of panic cycle, scholars in the 18th century had already gained some concepts. In the early 19th century, the merry-go-round-style law of panic cycle was highly advocated. But the spiral-style law of panic cycle was not invented until the end of the 19th century. But the current orthodox school is still applying the merry-go-round-style law of panic cycle from the early 19th century, so I want to correct it. The word "we" in my writing naturally refers to "our school", not to me personally.

The Problem of "Rationalization of Production" and "How to Struggle" 178

丨Letter from Mr. Zhu Ying丨

I have participated in the discussion of Mr. Weng Chongshi's question several times before and after. On the first day of this month, Mr. Shen Yimin gave some explanations to my so-called "rationalization of production", and I wanted to write a letter to answer. But because of the inconvenience of things, it was put on hold. Today I read Mr. Weng's letter again, and he wants to discuss directly with us. So I wrote this letter in the falling snow, enduring the bitter cold, to make separate replies.

First, I am replying to Mr. Shen. Of course, most of everything Mr. Shen explained is correct, but my so-called "As a result of the rationalization of production, you are exhausted all day long and cannot get enough to eat," there is nothing wrong with this sentence, and it does not conflict with what Mr. Shen explained, why? Mr. Shen explained that it is difficult to have four points, but the content is only to produce a large number of raw products with extremely little labor time and material energy. Do you know whether a worker has enough time under these conditions? Is it necessary to increase the speed of the machine and increase the intensity of the work? On the other hand, the faster the production speed, the more excessive the raw products, which leads to economic panic, and the capitalist's method of relief is to close factories, lay off workers, reduce wages, etc... From this point of view, "As a result of the rationalization of production, you are exhausted all day long and cannot get enough to eat." This sentence can be established. Naturally, the result of "rationalization of production" is not only this. But taking out a part of its results, logically, it does not violate any rules. As for "I am afraid that Mr. Zhu will also hate and oppose the rationalization of production in the current society and the rationalization of production in the future rational society," the basis for Mr. Shen's words is "The planned economy of the Soviet Union also reveals this clue," in other words: The economic organization of the Soviet Union is also implementing "rationalization of production." Regardless of whether this term seems to have not been heard in the Soviet Union, even if it is called "rationalization of production" in the future, the freedom and equality of capitalism are completely different from the freedom and equality of socialism. So we are now proposing "rationalization of production," there is no doubt that it refers to the economic organization of capitalism. Secondly, what I want to say to the reporter is: "Mr. Zhu is sick,..." and I don't have time to do a calm and precise analysis," or the reporter means to protect my shortcomings, I am of course grateful, but in fact I am not sick, no. I have never been sick, even in the "oppression of the capitalists". Attached with a smile.

Second: Reply to Mr. Weng. The reporter has answered Mr. Weng's letter in great detail. Now I want to say one more thing here, which is: 1. Choose a goal. The reporter said: "As long as you can know the source of your suffering, you can get it," this sentence is worthy of our appreciation. We must know who is giving us pain in the current society, and we must overthrow him. Who is giving us happiness, we must support him: look at which part of the world is a painful society, which part is a happy society, and it is not difficult to infer, and we must know that there is a kind of person among the two who is deceiving us with improved methods, and we must not follow them, and in fact, it has been proved that these people are often on the opposite side of us. 2. Establish a foothold. In the process of a person's struggle in society, not only can he not be understood by the general public, but even his closest relatives, sons, brothers, wives, etc., cannot be understood. Here, we can see a person's personality. Some people may be able to jump out of this environment, and some people will fall with them. It is best if we can learn from Liu Ling's drinking. His wife persuaded him to quit drinking. He agreed verbally, but in fact, he tricked him into drinking wildly once again. It is still five斗one石 to not listen to "women's words" (of course, educated women are excluded). Like the views of Mr. Weng's wife, it is naturally not surprising; but Mr. Weng should not only be influenced by her at this time, but should also insist on his own "Three Commandments", no, when he moves from a passive personal cultivation to a positive social reform in the future, his wife may interfere even more, then Mr. Weng should fight her even more. 3. Believe in yourself. As long as you have the right goal, as long as your position is firm, then you must believe in yourself. Because there are some people who see a great cause, especially a cause of reforming society, and feel that they are too small to achieve it. In fact, I am a member of society. I do my part, and others do their part. When combined, they become a great force. At the same time, with my firm struggle, I can influence others' firm struggle. "A nine-story platform starts with a pile of earth." As long as we do it bit by bit, the bright world can be achieved by people who others see as worthless today.

In addition, Mr. Weng wants us to tell him our mailing address. Since the reporter has introduced us, we may communicate with him directly in the future, or communicate through this newspaper. It is best to communicate through this newspaper, because firstly, our personal problems are everyone's problems, and secondly, getting the reporter to participate in the discussion will be of great help to us, and I think the reporter will agree.

Chaozhou Fellow-Villagers Association Requests Careful Discussion to Resolve the Method of Sealing Enemy Goods 184

The Chaozhou sojourning-in-Shanghai Fellow-Villagers Association, in light of the 9/18 Incident and the subsequent sealing of enemy goods in Shantou, valued at over ten million silver dollars, for which no proper resolution has been determined, leading to impacts on finance and endangering the social economy, yesterday specifically sent letters to the Shantou City Party Department, the Municipal Government, the Chamber of Commerce, and the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association. The letter stated: "Japanese invaders are running rampant, occupying our northeastern territory. The nation is engaging in economic severance with them, hence the act of sealing enemy goods. However, while the goods originate from an enemy country, the capital comes from numerous merchants. If we merely engage in sealing without seeking appropriate resolutions, the losses will not be limited to merchants alone, but will also impact the social economy. Therefore, various places in Shanghai and Guangdong have all established methods. While these methods differ, they all aim to eliminate the root causes without hindering the economy as the standard. We hear that since 9/18, Shantou has sealed enemy goods valued at over ten million yuan, but due to differing opinions, a method of disposal has been long delayed. Many businesses are implicated and going bankrupt, and the market is also panicking as a result. Furthermore, in recent years, over 300,000 overseas Chinese merchants from Chaozhou and Shantou, who have lost their jobs due to real estate and industry issues, have returned to their hometowns, reducing remittances by over 30 million yuan. Finance is stagnant, the market is depressed, and banditry is rampant, with no end in sight to the subsequent disasters. Therefore, we specifically send this letter, requesting investigation and hoping that you will immediately convene meetings of all sectors, with the main objectives of relieving losses and preventing drift. Regarding the sealed enemy goods, investigate and clarify the dates of import before 9/18, after 9/18, and after 1/28, and discuss appropriate sales methods separately so that the goods are not left to rot and finance can circulate, both to alleviate market panic and to prevent the re-entry of enemy goods. Otherwise, economic panic will endanger society, and Chaozhou and Shantou will inevitably descend into banditry. We hope you will adopt our suggestions and provide a reply."

Health Magazine Skin Special Issue: The fifth issue, the skin special issue, of Health Magazine, edited by Zhang Ziying, a national physician from Fudeli, Nancheng Road, is now published. Famous Doctor of Xiyi Passes Away: Yang Yiqing, a famous internal medicine doctor in Wuxi, has been practicing medicine for over thirty years, saving countless lives. He is also compassionate, waiving medical fees and even providing financial assistance for poor and sick patients. His dedication to helping the world without seeking fame or wealth is greatly admired by the people of the city. It is learned that Mr. Yang recently suffered a stroke after returning from treating patients, and despite medical treatment, he passed away. The local Chinese medicine community and general patients were saddened by this news.

The book is divided into twenty-two categories, with prefaces to the rules of each industry written by Wang Xiaolai, Xu Jiqing, Lin Shuhou, Xu Yongzuo, Pan Xulun, Zhou Zubo, Chen Zhirui, Dai Xisheng, Cai Yibai, Yan Yinwu, and others. The book is published by the Xinsheng News Agency Publishing Department at No. 280 Wangping Street, priced at one yuan and five dimes. The pre-order price is one yuan. Originally scheduled to be published on February 1, due to the end-of-year accounting period, the printing house has stopped working and will be delayed until February 10. In order to benefit readers, the agency will continue to offer the special price for pre-orders placed with the agency or the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce Commercial Monthly Agency before the book is published.

Letters to the Editor 189

To the esteemed editors of the Shen Bao: I am writing regarding the news item published in your newspaper's local news column on the 22nd of this month, concerning the Hengxingtai Oil Mill's carelessness, where the machinery, oil, factory foundation, and buildings were all reduced to ashes, resulting in losses of hundreds of thousands. This is completely untrue. While our factory did suffer a fire that evening, it was only a portion of the hulling machine and grinding room. Fortunately, it was still early, and the fire was quickly extinguished by the fire brigades from various districts. There were no major losses. Fearing the spread of misinformation, we specifically write to correct this. Please publish this correction in the correction column to reflect the true situation and avoid misunderstandings. Thank you very much. Sincerely, Hengxingtai Oil Mill Co., Ltd. January 22nd.

Ministry of Education Meeting on Secondary School Regulations 194

The Ministry of Education recently held a meeting on primary school regulations, and a general decision has been made. It will be officially announced after the review by the Deputy Ministers. The compilation of civic training materials for primary schools has been completed by the responsible department and submitted to the Minister for review. The announcement is expected to be soon. After the draft of the secondary school regulations was completed, a meeting was held on the 19th, passing one-third of the regulations. The meeting continued on the 21st, and two-thirds have been discussed. It will be completed soon. After the secondary school regulations are completed, the regulations for normal schools and vocational schools will be discussed. The Legislative Yuan has passed the Teacher Training Law, which does not include the status of rural teachers. There are currently 559 rural normal schools in various provinces and cities. Many schools have petitioned the Ministry of Education because the Teacher Training Law does not include the status of rural teachers. In order to provide relief, the Ministry of Education has included the status of rural teachers in the normal school regulations. After the resolution, the Ministry of Education will present the facts for remedy.

Zhejiang University Accepts Transfer Students for the Provincial Senior Agricultural School 196

National Zhejiang University is accepting transfer students for the first grade of Zhejiang Provincial Senior Agricultural School. The quota is 15 students for the agronomy department and 12 students for the forestry department. To be eligible to apply, applicants must have completed one semester at a public or registered private school of the same level as the senior agricultural school. When registering, applicants must fill out the registration form, submit an official transfer certificate and transcript, and two recent 4-inch half-length photos. The registration fee is one yuan. The examination subjects are Party Ideology, National Language, Mathematics (Higher Algebra and Trigonometry), English, Physics, Chemistry, Economics, Geology and Mineralogy, Biology, and Physical Examination. Applicants for the forestry department will be tested on Jurisprudence and Instrument Use. Registration starts on February 3rd and ends on the 6th. The examination will be held from the 7th to the 9th. The location is the Secretariat of Zhejiang University, University Road, Hangzhou.

Zhu Jiahao Gives a Speech, Ministry of Education Stops the Southwest from Changing the School System, and the Education Reform Plan is Under Review by the Standing Committee

There Are Students in North China Who Have Left School, but Not Many 197

Zhu Jiahao, Minister of Communications and concurrently Minister of Education, told a reporter from the Central News Agency yesterday that the Ministry of Education is still under his responsibility before Weng Wenhao takes office. Since he resigned as Minister of Education, the Central Government appointed Weng Wenhao as his successor, but Mr. Weng has been staying in Beiping for some matters and has not yet taken office, while he has not yet handed over the position. Therefore, he must continue to be responsible in fact. The Education Reform Committee of the Southwest Political Affairs Committee previously announced without authorization the abolition of winter and summer vacations, the reduction of the school year for universities and schools of all levels by one year, the division of one school year into four semesters, and a one-week vacation at the end of each semester. This is actually destroying the unity of the national school system. The Ministry of Education has sent a telegram to stop it. Some students in various schools in North China have left school without authorization, citing the tense situation, but not as many as reported in the newspapers. The Ministry of Education has sent a telegram to strictly stop it. As for the schools that have advanced their holidays, the Ministry of Education will give them appropriate punishment. The education reform plan proposed by Chen Guofu at the Third Plenary Session of the Central Committee is currently under review by the Standing Committee. Some of the points listed in the plan have already been implemented by the Ministry of Education, which has been detailed in the work report of the Ministry of Education. As for the rumor that the Labor University will be revived, it is absolutely untrue.

Professors from Universities in Beijing and Tianjin Go to the Front Line for Inspection 198

Hold a General Meeting After Returning to Beijing to Discuss Anti-Japanese Steps

Citizens of Beijing Ask the Central Government to Transfer Education Funds to Military Expenses

(Special Telegram from Beiping) After the loss of the Yuguan Pass, students from national and private universities in Beiping launched anti-Japanese movements, urging those who had fled to leave Beiping. Because the teaching staff was busy supervising and grading exams during the winter vacation, they did not show any anti-Japanese movement. The Standing Committee decided on the 18th to actively assist the delegation of volunteer troops. It was originally planned to go to the front line on the 19th to comfort the soldiers, but due to the problem of contacting vehicles, it was changed to the 20th. At the same time, 365 citizens of Beiping, including Chen Duxue, submitted a petition to the Central Government, requesting that the educational funds during the school suspension period of national universities be used for anti-Japanese military needs. The situation of all parties is recorded as follows:

Temporary Emergency Meeting 199

The delegation of the Joint Association of Teachers and Staff of National Colleges and Universities in Beijing and Tianjin held a temporary emergency meeting at Dongxinglou on the morning of the 19th. Those present were Wang Jixu, Yang Likui, Li Jianxun, Mou Tan, Liu Kuo, Jia Chengzhang, Xu Zhi, Liu Shichuan, etc. Wang Jixu presided over the meeting and passed the following items: 1. Publicly elect Wang Jixu and Yang Likui as the chief representatives to contact the military sub-committee for vehicles. 2. The comfort items have been purchased, including 1,000 pairs of velvet rope thick socks from Huaxing Hosiery Factory, and it was decided that the representatives will carry them to the front to distribute to the soldiers. 3. The period of comforting the soldiers is tentatively set for two days, which may be extended if necessary.

Wang Jixu Talks About the Mission 200

The reporter specifically visited Wang Jixu, a representative of the Teachers' Association, at about 3 pm on the 19th to inquire about the mission to the front line and the contact situation in Beijing. The main points of his speech are recorded as follows: Our association held a temporary standing committee meeting yesterday and decided to assist the soldiers fighting on the front line. First, Yang Likui, Mou Tan, Jia Chengzhang, Liu Kuo, Xu Zhi, Liu Shichuan, Li Jianxun, and I were elected as representatives to comfort the soldiers fighting against Japan on the front line. The eight representatives, upholding the public teachings, contacted all parties and prepared to go to the front line immediately. Mr. Yang (Likui) and I went to the sub-committee of the Military Commission today to contact the vehicle problem. According to the person in charge, "There are few vehicles and it is very crowded. I will convey your association's intention to Chairman Zhang (Xueliang) and will reply by telephone tonight (19th)." After we withdrew, we believed that we could only change the travel date. After consideration, it was changed to tomorrow (20th). The mission of our association's representatives to the front line this time has three: 1. Carry comfort items to comfort the soldiers fighting against Japan. 2. Inspect the battle situation on the front line. 3. Investigate the military supplies needed by the soldiers fighting against Japan. As for the anti-Japanese proposals in the general meeting of all teachers and staff, they will be decided after inspecting the situation on the front line.

Suspension of Education Expenses Presented 201

Chen Duxue and 365 other citizens of Beiping, because after the loss of Yuguan, students from various schools in Beiping did not engage in active anti-Japanese movements, but fled Beiping, which is contrary to the original intention of the country to cultivate students. During this school suspension period, the schools should no longer receive the education expenses from the state and the people's blood and sweat. They should be transferred to the anti-Japanese military needs to protect the country and shine the nation. The citizens today (18th) sent a telegram to the Kuomintang Central Committee, the Executive Yuan, and the Ministry of Education of the Central Government, requesting the suspension of education expenses during the school suspension period and the transfer to anti-Japanese military needs. The original text is recorded on the left: "We present a request to suspend the education expenses of national schools in Ping City during the school suspension period and transfer them to anti-Japanese military needs. Since the fall of Yuguan, the whole country has been shocked. The Japanese bandits' ambition to invade Pingjin has been fully exposed. At this critical moment of national survival, it is time for our people to strive to save the country. Even the ignorant people have this heart, and those who usually pride themselves on being high-level intellectuals should set an example at this time, lead the people, and be the vanguard of anti-Japanese, so as not to fail the original intention of the country's cultivation. This is what is not necessary to say. How can the cannon in Yuguan make the students who are known for their patriotism so afraid and seem to have a great disaster over their heads, and all flee, treating their personal lives as Mount Tai, and treating the people and the country as grass, so-called school rules and exams can be abandoned and ignored, and the school authorities have no binding force and guidance. As a result, the school is empty, and the gate can be closed to sparrows. The sound of lying on the rails to petition in the past is no longer heard today. This phenomenon is deeply painful. Looking back at the soldiers on the front line who are fighting against Japan, they are in the midst of guns and bullets, bathed in the wind and rain, encouraging and fighting, and falling forward and following, putting their families aside and not cherishing their lives. What is the purpose? To fight for the country's personality and for the nation's survival. And how should we in the rear encourage and assist them to be the backing and comfort the loyal and brave? In fact, the so-called patriotic students, have not seen the shadow of the Japanese army, have first been afraid of an empty, I do not know what to say to explain, what face to face this country to sacrifice the soldiers? Check the country spent huge sums to establish schools, the original is to create talent, consolidate the national foundation, if now this is the student can not be their share, the teacher can not be their job, since the student can not be their share, the teacher can not fulfill their duties, then the talent created no way, how can the national foundation be consolidated, is the same as the original intention of the country to establish schools, is greatly contrary, the teachers and students how can they enjoy the most expensive fee from the state and the people's blood and sweat? This is the first reason to request the suspension of the school's education expenses during the suspension period. Since the students left the school, all administrative affairs have entered a state of suspension. Since the administrative affairs of the school have been suspended, the work of the staff should also cease. This is the second reason to request the suspension of the school's education expenses during the suspension period. Then the soldiers on the front line are in the midst of bitter cold, their clothes are single and thin, and their rations are insufficient, relying only on their hot blood. Therefore, instead of spending the country's money on useless places, why not transfer it to the urgent needs of the anti-Japanese, this should be the third reason to request the suspension of the school's education expenses during the suspension period. Moreover, the impact of the suspension of education expenses is, at most, a few teachers and staff in Ping City. If the anti-Japanese military needs are once lacking, the impact will be the future of the entire country and nation. And the teachers and staff in Ping City have many side businesses, and they will not be worried about the cold due to the suspension of education expenses. If the anti-Japanese soldiers are once suspended, they will have the worry of freezing to death and starving to death, and the country and the people will be lost because of it. What is the importance of its advantages and disadvantages, which is urgent and which is slow, this should be the fourth reason to request the suspension of the school's education expenses during the suspension period. In summary, for these four reasons, we have prepared a document to request the Ministry to transfer all the educational funds of the national schools in Ping City during the school suspension period to the anti-Japanese military needs, so as to meet the expectations of the living and comfort the souls of the dead. Then, those who are grateful are not only Duxue and others. On the verge of tears, we sincerely state our words and hope to be approved. We respectfully present to the Kuomintang Central Committee, the National Government Executive Yuan, the Ministry of Education, the Ministry of Finance, and 365 citizens of Beiping, including Chen Duxue, Liang Guilin, Chen Ruoyu, Wang Shaolong, Yu Zhisheng, Li Yaohua, Yang Jianqi, Zhao Puqi, Lin Xianzhang, and Huang Zhenghan. (The names are not listed) We respectfully present to the National Government, the Central Party Department, the Executive Yuan, the Ministry of Education, (Sent on the 19th)

The County Education Association Requests that the Area Near the County Seat Be Designated as a Pilot Compulsory Education Zone 204

In order to popularize mass education and literacy, the Shanghai County Education Association has requested that the area near the new county seat be designated as a pilot compulsory education zone, and has specifically drafted reasons and methods to be submitted to the Administrative Committee of the County Education Bureau for adoption. The reasons and methods are listed below: (Reasons) To promote local autonomy and improve people's lives, popularizing education is the ladder and foundation. Although there are no detailed statistics on the number of illiterate people in our county, it is at least 60% or more, especially among adults. Although schools have been established everywhere, it is ultimately difficult to achieve universal education due to adherence to customs and economic constraints. It is considered that receiving education is a duty that citizens should fulfill. It is appropriate to delineate areas, conduct pilot compulsory education research methods, so as to not be hindered. If considerable results are obtained, then promote it to other areas, and the number of illiterates in our county may be sharply reduced. The new county seat area has convenient transportation and is the focus of attention. It is most suitable to be designated as a pilot compulsory education zone. (Methods) 1) Investigation and Statistics: Investigate and count the number of illiterate people within two li of the new county seat, and classify them by adults and children for statistics. 2) Zoning: Delineate the area and erect signs. 3) Supervisor: A director will be established in the pilot compulsory education zone, concurrently held by the Director of the Bureau or a member of the Education Committee. 4) Facilities: The existing primary schools within the zone will be directly under the jurisdiction of the director, and social work or school-style educational facilities will be increased as appropriate. Teachers will be transferred from various county-affiliated agencies and organizations. 5) Time Limit: Hypothetically three years. 6) Expenses: Borne jointly by various county-affiliated agencies and organizations. (According to law, various agencies and organizations have the obligation to establish mass schools.)

Shanghai Education Bureau Establishes Primary School Education Experiment Research Association 205

In order to expand the scope of experimental work, the Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau will change the original [Primary School Problem Experiment Research Preparatory Committee] to [Primary School Education Experiment Research Association], and promulgated nine rules. It is learned that the association held its inaugural meeting and the first standing committee meeting at 2 p.m. on the 19th, convened by the Third Section and designated experimental research schools. In addition to the staff of the Third Section of the Education Bureau and the Supervisory Office, there were also 28 attendees from 19 municipal schools. First, the chairman reported on the spirit of the association and the future work path, and then discussed the work methods for the next semester. Each school will determine its group, and each group will also appoint a leading school to first draft the working outline of each group and submit it to the next standing committee meeting for approval, and then carry out the work in division of labor. It was also decided that health education will be the research center of each group in the next semester, in order to adapt to the Bureau's determination that health is the center of education this year, so that the spirit of each school's work can be concentrated and consistent, and the effect will be more significant. Before the meeting, the experimental section of the Third Section had already collected many experimental research questions from various schools, and according to the nature of the questions, they were classified into each research group for experimental research in division of labor.

Shen Bao Medical Weekly

A Bird's-Eye View of Medicine in Shanghai Over the Past Decade (Continued) 216

— Pang Jingzhou

Chapter 3: Business Situation

Adding some foreign official arrogance made the general public feel the dread of hospitals, even to the point of using hospitals to represent the face of foreigners. The Chinese-run hospitals, such as the Red Cross Hospital and the Shanghai Public Hospital, were small in scale and lacked economic resources, and were unable to carry out much work. In the past twenty years, more labor hospitals and affiliated hospitals of several medical schools have appeared. Together with the small-scale public hospitals outside the city, there are no fewer than twenty or thirty. I will now list the Shanghai Public Hospitals in the table below, and note their nature, departments, and scale for readers to refer to. However, omissions are inevitable. If there are any omissions, please point them out.

The so-called scale in the table is based on the average calculation of houses and equipment. Among the levels of wards, the so-called high-level refers to ordinary people who cannot afford even their third-class ward, and the so-called middle-level refers to wards that are too simple and unrefined for the general capitalist class to live in. The so-called commoner is close to accepting only poor people, which ordinary middle-class people do not want to live in. Only those with all levels seem to be the most inclusive. However, the prices of wards also vary from hospital to hospital. Generally, the third-class ward costs more than five jiao per day, which makes the poor flinch. The second-class ward costs more than two yuan, which is considered expensive for middle-class people. Based on the above table, the following points can be distinguished: 1) Among the 30 hospitals listed, 12 are larger in scale, but 9 are foreign-run; 2) There are 7 hospitals specially set up for commoners, but 3 are for treating cholera, one is for obstetrics, and is unrelated to other diseases (However, the Emergency Plague Hospital provides daily consultation and medicine during non-cholera periods, without taking any fees.); 3) Among the 30 hospitals, only 3 have gynecology departments, and pediatrics is attached to gynecology. The number of beds is small, which can be imagined. If the number of children in the city is taken as a ratio, the difference is too great; 4) Although there are many obstetrics hospitals, there are very few with local public nature. This table only includes a moderate amount, but it is still insufficient.

Looking at the above points, the hospital situation in Shanghai can really be said to be still under deformity. To put it in a vulgar way, it is simply uneven. As for why there are so few public hospitals, there are also several reasons, which I will now discuss:

Scientific Essays on Achieving Longevity (3) 217

— Yu Songyun

㈤ Fetus

(A) First Half of Pregnancy... The fetus is very small and floats in the amniotic fluid. Its position changes frequently;

(B) Second Half of Pregnancy... The fetus grows larger and its position can no longer change, so there is a fixed fetal position;

(C) Normal Delivery... Normal delivery is also called spontaneous delivery, which accounts for about 99% of deliveries. It is divided into cephalic presentation (head down), breech presentation (buttocks down), and lower limb presentation (foot or knee down). Among these three, cephalic presentation is the most common, accounting for about 96%;

(D) Transverse Lie... This means that the diameter of the fetus crosses with the diameter of the uterus, accounting for about 1%. The common saying that the fetus must turn its head during delivery is completely untenable;

(E) Posture... The fetus has a fixed posture in the uterus during the second half of pregnancy, taking a Turkish sitting position, with the head bent forward towards the chest, the back curved, the upper limbs crossed in front of the chest, and the lower limbs bent forward towards the upper abdomen;

(F) Fetal Nutrition... In the first three weeks of pregnancy, the ovum has its own inherent nutrition. In the fourth week, the decidua absorbs nutrients. After the umbilical cord tissue is established, it is transported by the blood vessels in the umbilical cord. Most of the fetal excrement is also transported back to the mother's body through the umbilical cord;

(G) Fetal Movement... Starting from the fifth month of pregnancy, the pregnant woman feels the fetus moving in her abdomen. This is caused by the stretching and contraction of the fetus's trunk and limbs.

㈥ Pregnancy Status

(A) Various Signs are as follows:

(1) Previously regular menstruation suddenly stops;

(2) Frequent urination, because the uterus grows upwards during the second or third month of pregnancy, compressing the bladder;

(3) Nausea and vomiting, occurring around the second or third month of pregnancy, or even as early as the first month. It initially occurs in the early morning and is very common!

(4) The breasts become slightly swollen and distended from the second month of pregnancy, and they feel exquisitely sensitive. The areola pigment turns reddish-brown, and the nipples protrude. Between the fourth and fifth months, if you press on the breast, thin milk can be squeezed out;

(5) Abdominal enlargement. In the first month of pregnancy, the uterus is the size of a pigeon egg. In the second month, it is as large as a goose egg. In the third month, it is as large as a child's head. In the above three months, the uterus only enlarges in the pelvic cavity. The outside of the abdomen can already be clearly touched. By the fourth month, the uterus ascends and enters the abdominal cavity. By the fifth month, the uterus is level with the navel. By the eighth month, the bottom of the uterus is between the navel and the tip of the sternum. By the ninth month, the bottom of the uterus is at the tip of the sternum. In the tenth month, it bends forward towards the abdominal wall and lowers again, similar to the eighth month.

(B) Various Abnormalities are as follows:

(1) Pregnancy Line... In multiparous women during the ninth or tenth month, faint red or purplish-red streaks appear on the skin of the abdomen. These are old scars from previous pregnancies;

(2) First Perception of Fetal Movement... The pregnant woman first feels fetal movement in the abdomen around the fourth or fifth month (20th week);

(3) Uterine Contractions... If you place your fingers on the bottom of the uterus of a pregnant woman's abdomen, you will feel that the area being pressed changes from slightly hard to harder, and then gradually softens again, but it cannot be determined whether she is pregnant or not;

(4) Changes in Reproductive Organs... The mucous membranes of the vulva and vagina are thicker than usual and turn into distinct purple wrinkles. The muscles around the vulva proliferate, and the vulva cavity expands and lengthens. The labia majora sometimes show enlarged veins;

(5) Vaginal secretions are more abundant than usual, and the temperature is also higher;

(6) Cervix... Softer than usual. In the early stages of pregnancy, the cervix is light purple. By the end of pregnancy, it is blue. The cervical shape is shorter;

(7) Pelvic Joints... During pregnancy, the pelvic joints can relax, and during childbirth, the joints can move slightly;

(8) Heart Changes Position... When the uterus enlarges, it presses all the abdominal organs backwards, or to the sides or upwards, pushing the diaphragm upwards, causing the heart to move from its original position;

(9) Varicose Veins... During the second half of pregnancy, varicose veins often appear on the legs and anus (hemorrhoids). If they already exist, they will worsen at this time;

(10) Lung Compression... When the abdomen is very distended, the diaphragm presses upwards, causing the lungs to be compressed, and the shoulders move when breathing;

(11) Nervous System... The pregnant woman's nerves are disturbed by pregnancy, her temperament changes, and she sometimes experiences symptoms such as toothache, headache, bone pain, and dizziness. Her preferences also often change, and she experiences unpredictable joy, anger, worry, and depression. Some women are also mentally agile and very lively;

(12) Digestive System... In addition to nausea and vomiting, there are also drooling, spitting, heartburn, and constipation;

(13) Systemic Changes... Sometimes the body is healthier than usual after conception. Sometimes there are systemic changes, which are very complex. Sometimes they are discovered at the beginning of pregnancy, and sometimes they are discovered at the end, but they should not be considered diseases. However, the intensity of the changes varies from person to person;

(14) Abnormal Skin Pigmentation... In addition to the areola turning purplish-brown, dark circles appear under the eyelids, and yellow or brownish-purple spots appear on the midline of the face, forehead, neck, and abdomen. Even beautiful women often change color;

(15) Swaying Posture... Because the abdomen protrudes forward, the pregnant woman bends her upper body backwards to maintain her center of gravity, so even though she is hunchbacked when walking, it is like this.

Page 14

Good Medicine in Our Eyes and Good Medicine in General Eyes 218

— Wang Qizhang

In the first issue of this magazine, I mentioned good doctors in our eyes versus good doctors in the public's eyes. I received favorable feedback from readers, who believe that the current social chaos and lack of intellectual discernment have created opportunities for troublemakers, making the social situation even darker, which is truly heartbreaking. However, I believe that the mixture of transitional eras is a common principle in the world. Because the changes and evolution of everything have stages, and with stages, there will be succession. During succession, various incomplete phenomena and abnormal things will inevitably occur. Therefore, our current society is in a period of change and evolution, and of course, various strange and unexpected things will occur. However, the individuals during the period of succession cannot exhibit the same stage because their rates of change and evolution are different. For example, we are also a member of the current society. Why are our views different from those of the general public? This is related to the rate of change and evolution. Didn't I say last time that the distance in intellectual concepts between individuals in our Chinese society today spans two to three thousand years? In the same era and society, when intellectual concepts are so far apart, it is inevitable that there will be a sense of "us" versus "them."

Now, I want to talk about the intellectual concept of medicine. Medicine is originally a substance used to treat diseases. Anything that can achieve the goal of treating disease is good medicine, and anything that cannot is not good medicine. This seems like a very simple question. What difference is there between "us" and "them" in this regard? That's right, but the term "good medicine" is very difficult to make in reality. There are things that are truly good medicine but have not been verified, there are relatively good medicines that still need to be improved, there are things that are good medicine but whose usage is unclear, and there are many so-called good medicines, advertised good medicines, and whatnot good medicines. The degrees of superiority and inferiority and the differences in understanding are truly up to individual judgment, and it is difficult to say everything in one word. Whether or not the goal of treating disease can be achieved may not have a true or false standard. It is difficult to avoid the murmuring of the people of Chu, so it is inevitable that Qu Yuan would lament the worthlessness of common things, and the question of whether or not good medicine is truly good medicine ultimately falls into a fog.

In our eyes, the good medicine we currently hope for and recognize is not satisfied simply because it can cure one or a few people's illnesses. The true quality of medicine must meet each of the conditions written below. The good medicine we consider must first supplement or suppress the local abnormal mass that caused a disease and restore it to its original state. In other words, it restores the original anatomical mass, not the physiological function. For example, in the case of stroke, we know it is a brain hemorrhage. If we can restore the changes in the brain to their original state, then the stroke will naturally be cured. Also, for example, in the case of diabetes, we know it is a change in the islet tissue of the pancreas. If we can restore the abnormal state, then diabetes will naturally be completely cured. Medicines that can resolve this type of anatomical change are the highest-grade good medicines in our eyes. The next best thing is medicines that restore local physiological function without affecting other parts of the body. For example, in the case of stomach pain, the physiological abnormality is limited to the stomach. When we use painkillers, it is important to use local painkillers. In other words, it is only appropriate if it only stops the stomach pain and does not affect other parts of the body that are not in pain. Currently, the use of local anesthetics such as cocaine is considered the best, but these types of drugs, when absorbed into the body, can cause many side effects. As for morphine and related drugs that numb everything with one injection, and tetrodotoxin that paralyzes nerve endings, these common anesthetic drugs are even lower grade. Also, for example, digitalis has a special effect on the heart muscle, and atropine has a special effect on the pupillary sphincter muscle. The same muscle, yet its effect is particularly significant, which is indeed a valuable medicine. However, side effects are still unavoidable. Therefore, we hope very much that medicines that restore local physiological function will not affect other parts of the body. Only then can they be considered second-grade good medicines. As for bactericidal drugs, they can also be considered an important type of medicine for controlling pathogens. However, there are many bactericidal drugs for external use, but not many bactericidal drugs for internal use. This is because internal sterilization must take into account the need to avoid harming the host. If a drug has bactericidal power, it may also kill somatic cells. Therefore, it is difficult to find drugs that are more toxic to bacteria and less toxic to somatic cells. For example, salvarsan is weakly toxic to somatic cells and strongly toxic to bacteria. Also, quinine is weakly toxic to somatic cells and strongly toxic to sporozoa. There are also various animal immune serums that are weakly toxic to somatic cells and strongly toxic to various infectious bacteria. These types of drugs are rare today, and they are not satisfactory. It is quite difficult to find a good medicine that is strongly toxic to pathogens and non-toxic to somatic cells. If there is such a medicine, it can be considered a third-grade good medicine in our eyes. In addition, there are many medicines that have many effects, and the medicine with the strongest effect is considered the main medicine. There are countless names and complex formulas, but in reality, aren't they just modified versions of the same substances? These types of drugs are the most commonly used today, and doctors struggle the most to thoroughly solve diseases. It wouldn't be too harsh to classify them as fourth or fifth grade, would it? Therefore, the first-grade good medicines in our eyes can restore the abnormal anatomical mass, the second-grade can restore the local physiological function, and the third-grade is only for substances that kill pathogens in the body. Other medicines that repair trivial parts and the most common symptomatic medicines can only be classified as fourth or fifth grade.

As for the good medicine in the eyes of the general public, that is completely different from our understanding. Their central judgment is dominated by their ears and eyes. The efficacy of their good medicine is completely dictated by their state of mind. Therefore, their good medicine is propaganda-based medicine, psychological medicine, and it can almost be said to be completely unrelated to the original purpose and function of medicine. For these types of medicines, whether it's sand, incense ash, or any kind of grass root or tree bark, nothing is bad. Therefore, all kinds of bizarre things are heavily advertised and fill our Divine Land, dazzling our eyes and ears, and almost no one can tell the difference between east, west, south, and north. However, having said that, there are still high and low grades among the medicines that the general public considers good. Because the good medicines of the general public are originally over-the-counter medicines, in other words, folk remedies. The nature of these types of medicines is to fit the medicine to the disease, not to fit the medicine to the disease according to the prescription of a doctor. Therefore, they have different tendencies from the symptomatic medicines prescribed by doctors. However, among over-the-counter medicines, there are also things that conform to scientific principles and are indeed scientific products, and are welcomed and used by doctors. However, the majority are off track or are completely deceptive forgeries, deceiving the public who lack medical knowledge, and aiming to absorb the money of women and the poor. Comparatively better ones have similar efficacy and quality, but they are always exaggerations. The lowest grade ones say one thing about efficacy and another thing about quality, mixing things up and talking nonsense. That's really terrible. Recently, I saw an advertisement saying that there is a type of domestic medicine called something-something-su, which he claimed had 2 million times the powerful phlegm-resolving and cough-suppressing power. When mathematics talks about multiples, there must first be a unit. I don't know how to calculate this unit of phlegm-resolving and cough-suppressing efficacy. If there is no unit and it is called 2 million times, isn't that a huge joke? For example, the efficacy of this type of medicine is too far off or completely opposite, and some people who are deceived and anesthetized by it may consider it a kind of good medicine, which is not known. There are also what grass, what essence, what pills, powders, ointments, and elixirs for days and nights. What he advertises and attracts are people who are outside the medical world. What he squeezes and induces is the money of general pitiful people. These pitiful people still think they are extremely clever and can choose the world's most advanced magic medicine to bring the dead back to life, which is truly pitiful to the end. I used to investigate the standards for managing over-the-counter medicines in various countries overseas. There are differences in the strictness of his standards. Some must be effective for a certain disease to be considered qualified, and some only require that they be non-toxic and do not harm physiology to be considered qualified. However, at least there is the restriction that the prescription and medicine must match, and the efficacy must not deviate from the medicine. Therefore, the law of medicine advertising is very important and very strict. Alas, in our current situation, I don't know where to start. I can only put down my pen here.

The Urgent Need to Advocate for Domestic Medicines is a Reaction to the Correction of Non-Scientific Medicine 219

— Hu Dingan

In the world, everything has a cause and then a result; has an object and then a motive; and then generates a reaction. We know the warlords abuse and harm the people. Therefore, there is a national revolution. We know the economic oppression, so we must resist capitalist aggression! Is it not the same with academic matters? We have seen the absurdities of non-scientific medicine and the deceptions of a kind of non-scientific medicine that has recently been on the sea. For the sake of the future of Chinese medical science, we are compelled to rise up and carry out this scientific movement to advocate for domestic medicines because of this reaction.

We have seen that the Western medicines and Chinese medicine shops from foreign countries are leaking large quantities every year, which affects the entire national economy dangerously. At the same time, we have seen that some people in the country want to do some speculative deals in response to the trend, but they cannot create domestic medicines according to scientific methods. They can only rely on advertising to deceive Chinese compatriots, and they can only deceive compatriots who have no medical knowledge. The scientific foundation has lost its center of gravity. This kind of advocacy for non-scientific medicines and the parallel fallacies and errors of non-scientific medicine have the same direction. Originally, advocating for domestic medicines is a very good thing, but using domestic medicines without creating them according to scientific methods is just superficially reclaiming rights and can replace the functions of imported goods. This kind of non-scientific medicine is really not the original intention of what we want to advocate for creating scientific domestic medicines. Because this cannot achieve academic progress, it is not a thorough solution. Therefore, in order to catch up quickly and meet the current urgent needs, all medical colleagues in the country should completely use scientific methods to select several kinds of domestic medicines that should be created first, or several kinds that have already been registered, and manufacture them according to pharmaceutical procedures. We must establish a solid scientific foundation and then seek other kinds of accomplishments. Pharmacists should obtain the main components from the analytical aspect and apply pharmacology to animal experiments. Medical scientists should use the pharmacological aspect to identify the therapeutic functions of drugs. Some people cannot report the main components that have been analyzed at one time, so they can continue to study them successively. It seems that we can first conduct experiments on several kinds that we are already sure of in advance, get the results, and then manufacture them first. We must indeed obtain the true evidence that can be reported in the scientific community from the conscience before we can create a certain drug for application to humans as a therapeutic drug. Of course, non-scientific medicine is popular in society, does not cure diseases, and does not send people to their deaths, which is not necessarily a very serious problem. If there are no scientifically based reports internationally, the academic community will not have the slightest impact, or they will cover up all the weaknesses with secret prescriptions and secret preparations and follow suit, then they can apply it to various drugs. If it contains very violent components, they will also think that it is not important, and they will create it vaguely, I am afraid that it will definitely lead to very large abuses and dangers. From this point of view, the scientific method of pharmaceutical manufacturing, using domestic medicines to manufacture medicines, has a certain procedure, a certain pharmaceutical procedure, and more scientific research, which can also be regarded as the minimum standard when we advocate for domestic medicines and plan to create them. I hope that the colleagues in the new medical field will actively think about creating domestic medicines in order to reclaim rights and promote scholarship. I also think that it is the duty of a citizen to participate in the work of advocating for domestic medicines if the old medical community can recognize the general trend and jump out of metaphysics and move into the scientific community to surrender. Chinese medicine shops should also supply materials and help accomplish the great cause. What is called science to save the country, in this critical moment, with scientific knowledge, using scientific methods, and creating domestic medicines, is not it a very clear fact?

Idle Chat After Diagnosis (2) 220
