Economic Special Issue

A Glimpse into the Recent Decline of Major Products in Jiangxi Province 221

Widespread banditry leads to the collapse of the rural economy.

Production experiences a major setback, and exports plummet.

Jiangxi Province is rich in products, among which porcelain, wood, tea, paper, and ramie cloth are the mainstays of the province's import and export trade. The total trade value annually reaches 30 to 40 million yuan. In recent years, banditry has spread throughout the province, and local products have declined daily. The rural economy has collapsed accordingly, and the poverty of the region is readily apparent. Here is a brief account of the recent situation of porcelain, tea, paper, and wood in Jiangxi Province, in order to illustrate the decline of major industries in Jiangxi.

Porcelain

Jingdezhen porcelain has always been renowned for its fine quality and precious value. For centuries, it has been praised without decline, not only being the best in the country but also well-known in the West. Before 1927, production was at its peak, with an average annual total value of about 10 million yuan. Its sales extended to Southeast Asia, Europe, and the Americas. Recently, according to a survey by the Porcelain Affairs Bureau, there are a total of 23 types of porcelain businesses, with 1,504 kiln factories, 22,029 workers, and a capital of 1,535,885 yuan. The total annual output value is 5,600,6151 yuan, a decrease of more than 4 million yuan compared to before 1927. There are two reasons for this decline. Before 1927, there were more than 70 large and small money houses in Jingdezhen, and the financial situation was active. If a porcelain merchant brought a town draft for 10,000 yuan to purchase porcelain, they could sell the draft to the money house. The money house only paid with a promissory note (from 100 to 2 yuan), which could be cashed at any time and circulated in the market, making transactions very convenient. Therefore, the money supply was smooth, and trade developed accordingly. After 1927, wars were frequent, and the financial situation was critical. Town drafts became ineffective, and the promissory notes issued by the money houses were also stranded and could not be discounted. As a result, credit was lost, and the market became difficult to circulate. Even the oldest and most reliable money houses reduced their business scope and became more cautious in lending. This is one reason for the decline of the porcelain industry due to economic distress. In recent years, Communist bandits repeatedly captured and plundered, causing significant damage to the porcelain industry. After the September 18th Incident, sales in the three northeastern provinces were completely blocked. Merchants from Yingkou, Harbin, and Guandong did not come. In addition, other provinces were difficult to transport to due to military blockades and traffic obstructions. This is another reason for the decline due to military and banditry influences. The former establishment of the Ceramic Industry Department, was determined to take on the responsibility of guidance and improvement of porcelain production, by setting up a Ceramics Department within the Bureau, to study the improvement of the porcelain industry, and set up a Ceramics Affairs Bureau in Jingdezhen, in addition to undertaking technical affairs, it is also responsible for all aspects of guidance of the porcelain industry. Since its establishment, although gradual results have been seen, there is still no thorough improvement. This spring, due to the impact of the Shanghai war, the money supply was extremely tight, and porcelain businesses were plagued by economic problems. In addition, the provincial government established a special bureau in Jingdezhen to collect porcelain taxes in order to handle the suppression of bandits, increasing the burden on porcelain merchants. In September, there was a strike and business suspension. Last month, the chairman of the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, Wang Xiao, and other porcelain industry representatives went to Jiangxi to request the authorities to abolish the tax and change it to a business tax, fixed at 440,000 per year. Compared to the year when porcelain production was at its peak, the burden on porcelain merchants has not been reduced. Moreover, since the Mid-Autumn Festival, it has been the off-season for porcelain sales, and most porcelain merchants from various provinces have returned home. Also, due to the approaching end of the year, the financial situation is extremely tight. In the past month, only a dozen kilns have been fired in Jingdezhen, and no one has asked about the porcelain products. The market is depressed, which is unprecedented in recent years. The future of the porcelain industry is not optimistic.

Tea

Jiangxi has always been the richest tea-producing area in the western part of the Yangtze River. Green tea from Dexing and Yushan, and black tea from Xiushui, Hekou, and Fuliang are the main exports of the province. In the heyday of tea production, Xiushui foreign-owned black tea companies had an annual output of 160,000 to 170,000 boxes, Hekou 20,000 to 30,000 boxes, Dexing also produced more than 20,000 boxes in 1928, and Fuliang more than 40,000 boxes. In the past ten years, Xiushui and Wuning black tea, initially because Russian sales were weak and prices were low, tea farmers suffered losses. Therefore, merchants from Anhui and Guangdong who came to the mountains to set up businesses have decreased year by year. Mountain households, because tea prices were low, mostly cut down tea trees and planted other crops. Those who did not cut them down also did not add manpower and fertilizer to the management and cultivation, so the quality gradually deteriorated. Foreign merchants who process tea mostly abandoned Ning Hong and preferred Qihong. In recent years, production has decreased even more sharply. This year, only a few local companies came to the mountains to set up businesses. Hekou black tea, because the quality is even worse than Ning production, foreign merchants have raised and lowered prices, and business is also stagnant. This year, there are only a few companies operating black tea in Hekou and three companies operating green tea in Yushan. The total output is only about 10,000 boxes, which is far less than ten years ago. Dexing green tea, because the production area borders Wuyuan, the quality is not bad. Two years ago, the output was still more than 10,000 boxes. Since last year, when the Communists occupied the area, it has become a bandit area. Farmers cannot harvest and process tea in time during the new tea growth period. Tea leaves are abandoned on the ground, and there has been no production for two years. Only Fuliang black tea relies on the reputation of Qimen and has managed to survive. However, this year, due to the tight money supply, tea firms have reduced their remittances, and fewer companies have set up businesses than in previous years. The produced tea is also subject to price suppression by foreign merchants, resulting in great losses. The fate of Fuliang tea is gradually narrowing, and it will show the same declining trend as Xiushui black tea. Recently, the Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau, in order to understand the actual situation of the decline of Xiushui tea, sent personnel to Jiangxi in April to investigate, and reported the improvement opinions to the Ministry of Industry. The plan to revive the tea industry is very thorough. Recently, Chairman Xiong, in view of the decline of Ning tea, will also organize a large-scale company to set up a factory in Jiujiang in order to save the endangered tea industry. If the above two facilities can be implemented, then Xiushui black tea still has a glimmer of hope. It is a gratifying news that Jiangxi's tea industry, which has fallen into a deep abyss, has been given a helping hand.

Paper

Jiangxi is located on the south bank of the middle reaches of the Yangtze River, with a mild climate and lush bamboo forests everywhere. The abundance of bamboo production is the highest in the country, so the development of its paper industry is also a natural trend. There are more than eighty counties under the jurisdiction of the province, and paper-producing counties account for more than half of the counties. Among them, the largest output is in the four prefectures of Ji'an, Ganzhou, , and , followed by the four prefectures of Yuanzhou, Guangxin, Fuzhou, and Jianchang. The areas with relatively large output are Shicheng, Taihe, and Yichun counties. There are more than 6,900 households engaged in papermaking in the province, with 30,000 workers. The types of fine paper include Lian Shi, Mao Bian, Xuan Paper, , Xin Pi Paper, Hu Guan Oil Paper, Biao Xin, and imitation Western paper, etc. Coarse paper includes Zhong Biao Xin, Hua Jian, Yuan Biao Xuan Biao, Mian , Ci Biao, Bi Zhou Ci Biao, Liang Kou Kun Biao, and Xiao Paper. Fine paper is mainly Mao Bian, Lian Shi, Gong Chuan, Zou Mu Bamboo Paper, Bai , and Pu Paper. The annual output of Mao Bian is about one million yuan, and the annual output of Lian Shi is about one and a half million yuan. The total output of other fine papers is about 500,000 yuan. Among coarse papers, the annual output of paper and fire paper is about 40,000 yuan. The annual output of fire paper concentrated in Wucheng, Fengxin, and Jing'an is about one million yuan. The total amount of consumption in other places is also 3 million yuan. According to a survey in 1918, the total output of coarse and fine paper in the province was 8,116,163 yuan. In recent years, Ganzhou, Fengxin, and Jing'an fire paper in North China have plummeted. The reason is that the manufacturing method has not been improved. Except for sacrificial purposes, it has no other uses. The area of the paper production in the province has not been peaceful for years, and transportation is difficult. The enthusiasm of those engaged in this industry is negative, and the output has decreased sharply. The sales volume in North China used to be about 3 million yuan, but now it is only hundreds of thousands of yuan. In addition, the Mao Bian and Lian Shi produced by machine-made paper mills in Shanghai are superior to Jiangxi products and the prices are cheaper. Those who used to use Jiangxi paper now mostly buy products from Shanghai factories. The sales market of Mao Bian and Lian Shi has also been taken over by Shanghai paper by half, so Jiangxi's paper industry will decline from now on, and it is difficult to restore its former prosperity.

Wood

Most counties in Jiangxi Province are mountainous and have always been famous for producing wood. The largest variety is fir wood from Ganzhou, Longnan, Ruijin, Shangyou, Chongyi, Suichuan, and other places in southern Jiangxi, followed by camphor wood. Fir wood produced in Ganzhou is the best, because the mountainous area upstream of Ganzhou is fertile, the climate is mild, and it is most suitable for planting wood. The produced wood is firm, slender, durable, and long-lasting. Except for the Guang wood produced in Changde, it can be called the best material of fir wood in our country. The largest sales volume is in Jiangsu Province, followed by various ports in the province and Wanwu. Exported wood is transported from the production area to Wucheng for centralized manufacturing and compiled into wooden rafts. After passing through Poyang Lake, it is directly released into Nanjing and unloaded into small rafts, then transported to Changzhou for sale. Changzhou is a centralized area for wood from Jiangxi and Hubei. Most of the wood sold is also produced in Jiangxi. The total annual sales value is about 7 million yuan, and the annual sales value in Wanwu and the province is about 8 million yuan. In terms of value, it has increased compared to the past. In terms of output, it has decreased compared to the past. In the early years of the Republic of China, the value of western wood was about ten coins. Now it has increased to forty or fifty coins. The value is four times that of the past. In recent years, most of the wood-producing counties in southern Jiangxi have been ravaged by bandits, and transportation is difficult. This year, Changzhou wood businesses, due to the decline of the silk industry in Jiangsu Province, the price of cocoons in various counties has not risen, and the economy of farmers is difficult, so they are unable to engage in construction. The demand for wood has been greatly reduced. In the past, each Changzhou company sold more than one million yuan of wood each year, but this year it is only 200,000 to 300,000 yuan. Those who operate western wood in Linjiang and Hui mostly hoard it and cannot sell it. The sales market of fir wood in Jiangsu Province this year has fallen into a sluggish state. Camphor wood is sold in the northern provinces and in the province for the manufacture of wooden furniture and leather boxes, but the output and sales volume are only one-tenth of fir wood, which is insignificant to the rise and fall of wood.

Ramie Cloth

Jiangxi's ramie production is very rich, and the output of ramie cloth is also more than other provinces. The largest production areas are Wanzai, Yifeng, Chongren, Fuzhou, and other counties, followed by Ningdu, Hekou, and Yushan counties. Its exports are sold in major commercial ports at home and abroad. The total annual value is about 5 million yuan. The quality of ramie cloth in various counties is the best in Wanzai, and it is called the best product in the country together with the products produced in Liuyang, Hunan. The overseas sales are mostly needed by the United States and Korea. For example, the Western tablecloths produced by Jiangxi Women's Handicraft Society are especially welcomed by Americans. However, in the past two years, most of the ramie cloth producing areas have become bandit areas, and men and women workers cannot work with peace of mind, and the output has decreased. The sales market in Korea has also been restricted by the Japanese government due to my country's boycott of Japanese goods. The sales volume has decreased sharply. This year, the production and sales volume of ramie cloth in various counties is only 40% of the previous year.

A Review of China's Silk Industry in the Past Year 222

— Zhao Dingyuan

In recent years, it has been a period of decline for China's silk industry. In the recent one or two years, the degree of its intensification has reached its extreme. The entire silk industry is in a precarious state of bankruptcy. From the silkworm-raising farmers at the bottom to the silk merchants at the top, as well as the silver and money industries that provide financial support, all are in a deep and painful situation and cannot extricate themselves.

Raw silk is the main commodity in China's international trade. Its failure affects all farmers, merchants, and workers engaged in the silk industry, which are closely related and cannot be exempted. Since the spread of the global recession, raw silk, which has the nature of a luxury item, has naturally been affected first. Overseas demand has suddenly decreased, and inventory cannot be sold. As a result, China's silk merchants and silk factories have been trapped in a stranded predicament. The silk cocoons mortgaged to the silver and money industries cannot be redeemed, and they have fallen into bankruptcy. The number of unemployed workers is increasing, and labor disputes have begun, and have become even worse since the January 28th Incident.

Silk merchants cannot redeem the mortgaged silk cocoons, and financial funds are greatly affected. On the one hand, they cannot continue to finance, and silk merchants are in more difficult situation. On the other hand, because cocoons cannot be stored for a long time, they have to find ways to process them on behalf of the silk factories, in order to avoid wasting resources and reduce losses. After the Shanghai war, a considerable number of silk factories eked out a living by processing old cocoons, which was a very miserable situation.

The decline of China's silk industry did not start today. It has attracted the attention of the whole country. The government and the public are competing to find a way out, such as organizing the Jiangsu and Zhejiang Old Factory Silk Sales Committee, and establishing the Jiangsu and Zhejiang Old Factory Silk Cocoon Committee. The government is also eagerly promoting and issuing public bonds, trying to remedy the situation. In the spring this year, the decline of the silk industry had little to do with ordinary silk merchants, but directly affected the silkworm-raising farmers. The farmers' meager funds could not withstand unexpected and significant blows. As a result, the voice of rural bankruptcy became tense, and social order was disturbed. The reason for this is that the silk merchants this year saw the slump in the overseas silk market, the excessive old inventory, and the inflexibility of the finance. They stood by and watched. The price of cocoons and silk (referring to local silk) fell sharply, almost unattended. Compared with the competition in previous years, it cannot be measured. The decline of the silk industry has been for many years, but last spring, the general silk merchants did not know that the world economic panic had reached this extreme, so they still widely searched and bought, and finally the silk merchants suffered too much loss. This spring, silk merchants learned from the failure last year and tried to tighten up, and the price of cocoons plummeted, and the farmers suffered. Therefore, in the declining silk market last year, merchants suffered, and this year, farmers suffered alone. Most farmers are poor, so how can they withstand the huge storm. As a result, the voice of rural bankruptcy has become a topic of conversation among foreigners. (Please refer to my article "Investigation Record of Zhili Lake Silk" in the 23rd issue of the 4th volume of the Industrial and Commercial Bi-Monthly).

The silk market in the first half of this year was very sluggish. Overseas telegrams demanded too low a price, so old silk stopped moving forward, intending to wait and see. But in July and August, the raw silk market in Lyon, New York, and other places suddenly became active, and the price of silk rose sharply. The export of raw silk in the five countries suddenly became enthusiastic. Therefore, the trade of raw silk in our country this year, on the whole, is better than in previous years. The following is based on the latest "Weekly Raw Silk Export Report" of the Raw Silk Inspection Office to illustrate the overview of the raw silk export trade this year.

Year Bales to Europe Bales to Asia and Bales to America Total Exports

Africa

1930 15,197 6,691 17,694 39,582

1931 8,495 4,800 11,287 24,582

1932 9,416 8,651 7,255 25,322

We examine the above figures. The total number of exports this year, although not as good as in 1930, is undoubtedly more than in 1931. This is of course due to the government's efforts to promote relief, such as decisively exempting the export tax of 30 customs taels per package, and more actively allocating subsidies, calculated at 100 taels per load. In addition, the Jiangsu and Zhejiang Old Factory Silk Sales Committee has been actively promoting sales to overseas markets in an organized manner, but the global recession is still shrouded, so although all parties have worked together, the effect is not very significant.

European countries such as France, Switzerland, and Italy have been old customers of China for hundreds of years, (Italy is also a silk-producing country, but its silk is better made than Chinese silk, so it sells it to the United States to seek huge profits, and at the same time supplements it with cheap Chinese silk,) they are quite trustworthy to Chinese silk, so orders are coming in continuously, and the export trade has an upward trend. The so-called Asia in the table actually refers to India. India is still in the hands of the British, and the industry is very young. The standard of living is relatively low, so high-quality white factory silk is not what they need, and cheap silk is in line with their tastes. According to the Zhenze silk merchants in the silk producing area, their orders are two or three bales or four or five bales at a time, rarely exceeding ten bales, but the telegrams are continuous, all year round. The biggest problem with silk is that the uniformity of the strip is not good, which is not suitable for mass production, but it is quite suitable for small-scale handicraft industry. India has not yet separated from the handicraft era, so India has become a major customer of silk.

However, sales have declined, and there are two reasons for this. ㈠ The country is a large-scale mechanical production, so uniformity is the most important thing, and there are very few in that can meet its uniformity of more than 80 points. Even if there are, the silk brands are chaotic and there are many names, so the number of the same silk brand is relatively small, and the order of two or three hundred bales each time is naturally difficult to pay. The lack of so-called standardization (Standardization) is the first reason. ㈡ Japan, in view of this situation, took the opportunity to seize the US market, and strove to improve all products, and must be in line with the needs of the United States. At the same time, it spared no effort in promotion and publicity, so 95% of the total raw silk consumption in the United States is occupied by Japan, and the remaining few are small numbers. Japan adopts a consolidation policy, which is the second reason.

Although this year is still in the midst of the global economic panic, the government and the public have been able to save the dying life to the greatest extent. From this point of view, if human power can be exhausted, the natural trend cannot be reversed. In the future, we should pay attention to ㈠ the problem of production technology, and ㈡ the problem of rational distribution. I will discuss it again.

Soviet Russia's Consumer and Production Cooperative Enterprises 223

— Lin Bingzhong

Lenin said, "[Only] cooperation and electrification can build socialism," and also said "[The] bright cooperative system allows the public to manage the means of production, allowing the proletariat to overcome the bourgeoisie, which is the socialist system." This is the reason why Soviet Russia's cooperative enterprise is expanding so vigorously.

When it comes to Soviet Russia's cooperative enterprise, we should of course first analyze its purpose. We know that every country in the world now has cooperative organizations, and their purpose is to sell products to maximize the profits of their members, or to allow members to buy goods at the lowest prices. It can be said that the establishment of cooperatives is entirely for the sake of its members. However, this is not the case with Soviet Russia's cooperative enterprise. Although cooperatives inevitably seek benefits for their members, the benefits of members are only the secondary purpose of Soviet Russia's cooperative enterprise. Its main purpose is to use it as a tool to reform the economy and society, so that it can conform to the plans and principles of the Russian political party. Therefore, rather than regarding Soviet Russia's cooperative organization as a part of the world's cooperative movement, it is better to call it an organ of the Soviet socialist system. Because it recognizes that cooperative enterprise is a tool for reforming the social economy, the Soviet Union's cooperatives are completely controlled by the Party, just like industry, trade, banking, and other enterprises are controlled by the state. The staff members inside the cooperative, the policies of the cooperative, etc., are all controlled by the Party.

There are many types of cooperatives in Soviet Russia, but the two most important are consumer and production cooperatives. They are now described separately below.

(A) Consumer Cooperative Enterprise

Consumer cooperative enterprise is the most important of all cooperative enterprises. In the fiscal year 1929 to 1930, the number of people in the cooperative reached 40,258,000, accounting for 24.8% of the total national population. All Soviet citizens who have not been deprived of their civil rights are eligible to become members. In theory, people are free to join or not. However, in reality, non-members face various disadvantages, such as restrictions on purchasing goods and higher prices. Therefore, the current trend is that almost everyone is becoming a member.

The shares of members were originally fixed. In 1924, they were set at five rubles. However, in recent years, the collection of shares has been based on the salary of the purchaser of the shares, that is, the amount of one month's salary is used as the amount of the shares, which is paid in installments. Even if members have already paid their shares, they must make up for this amount. This increases the burden on the people, but to preserve the various benefits of membership, the number of people joining the cooperative continues to increase. In the fiscal year 1928 to 1930, the shares had already increased to 100,000,000 rubles. Dividends are not distributed on a regular basis, because each member only has one share, and the dividend amount is extremely small, so there is no need to add a lot of trouble to the bookkeeping.

Consumer cooperative enterprise can also be divided into several parts: (1) Rural consumer cooperatives, (2) Urban worker consumer cooperatives, (3) Transportation worker consumer cooperatives. Each cooperative establishes several stores, and each store is interconnected, just like the Chain Stores in the United States.

The Central Purchasing Union, Centrosoyuz, is jointly organized by various consumer cooperatives. Its duties are extremely heavy and can be roughly divided into the following points:

(1) Representative organ of consumer cooperatives, and can also be said to be the leader of consumer cooperatives.

(2) Establish warehouses to store goods for each store.

(3) Set up machines to manufacture consumer goods such as bread, canned food, and soap for the use of the entire city's population.

(4) Purchase goods from foreign countries. The Central Purchasing Union now has the exclusive purchasing right for Soviet Russia's tea trade.

(5) Assign technical personnel to each cooperative and organize the accounting system of each cooperative.

(6) Provide financial assistance to cooperatives with weak strength.

Currently, the import of consumer goods into Soviet Russia is completely controlled by the Central Purchasing Union, which is sold by cooperative stores. The most important part of this is the catering department. The newest Soviet Russian residences do not have equipment or places for individual families to cook, so public restaurants and city kitchens are established in large numbers. These restaurants are all established by cooperatives.

The most important administrative department of the consumer cooperative system is the Party. This system is not jointly managed by members, but is completely controlled by the Party. Management personnel are also elected by the members, but the people elected must be within the list of candidates listed by the Party.

(B) Production Cooperative Enterprise

Soviet Russia's production cooperative enterprise is also very developed. We know that Soviet Russia's first Five-Year Plan was successful, and the progress of industry has been rapid. At least part of this credit should be attributed to the domestic production cooperatives. It can be said that there are three purposes of Soviet Russia's production cooperatives. The first purpose is to bring domestic small-scale industries into the orbit of socialism. Soviet Russia's industry takes a state-owned policy, so it does not allow the existence of independent factories or workers. They believe that when factories or workers are independent, they are all thinking of their own interests, and the road they take will inevitably conflict with the development of socialism, so they must find a way to eliminate them. The method of elimination is either to merge them into state-owned industries, or to organize cooperatives to socialize them. The second purpose is to solve the unemployment problem with production cooperatives. The more production cooperatives there are, the more developed industry will be, and the more workers will be added. This is a very obvious fact. The third purpose is to solve the problem of commodity panic. Of course, the first of these three purposes is in the most important position.

Production cooperatives also accept members as much as possible. In theory, whether to join or not depends entirely on the individual's freedom. However, in reality, non-members face various disadvantages. In January 1930, the government issued an order prohibiting the supply of raw materials to non-cooperative members and the purchase of their living products. In this way, non-members simply have no way to live, so they joined the cooperative one after another. On October 1, 1929, the number of members of production cooperatives reached 1,460,000. In the same year, the total value of goods produced by domestic production cooperatives was 2.424 billion rubles. The extent of development can be seen from this.

The basic unit of the production cooperative organization is called [Artel]. There is no limit to the number of members, whether it is five or six people, or more than a thousand people. The administrative organ is a committee, and the committee is usually made up of three people, one of whom is the chairman. Their duties can be divided into the following four types:

(1) Plan the sale of goods.

(2) Act as a representative of the Artel.

(3) Purchase raw materials.

(4) Manage all daily administrative matters.

The workers (that is, members) inside the Artel also have wages, which are paid either weekly or monthly, or calculated according to working hours. The amount of wages varies, but there is a maximum limit. No matter what, each worker cannot earn more than 500 rubles per month, nor can they earn more than the wages of the same type of work in state-owned enterprises. If there is to be a large profit, the Labor Exchange will have to find a way to add workers to this to share their wages.

Members of the Artel must pay a share fee. There is a minimum limit for the share fee. People with sufficient strength must contribute more when needed to give to the Artel. There is also interest on this type of lending, about 8% to 10%. If a member is unable to pay the share fee, they may temporarily not have to pay, and it will be gradually deducted from their weekly wages, about 5% to 15% each time, depending on the amount of wages. Profits are not distributed to members, but are used for the following four purposes:

(1) 25% is used as a special capital fund and deposited in the All-Russian Cooperative Bank to lend to other cooperative enterprises.

(2) 10% is paid as income tax.

(3) Fund for the development of the company itself.

(4) Build clubhouses to improve the lives of workers.

The Artels in various places are united to form local production cooperatives. These local cooperatives jointly organize a production cooperative, the United Congress, as a design and guidance agency. There is also an organization called the All-Russian Production Cooperative Federation, which specializes in purchasing raw materials, allocating bank credit, and selling products.

In conclusion, after discussing the consumer and production cooperative enterprises of Soviet Russia, we know that the cooperative enterprise of Soviet Russia is a tool to promote socialism, and everything is controlled by the Party. This is a fundamentally different point from the cooperative systems of various countries, and it is also a point that we should pay special attention to. Of course, the types of cooperative enterprises in Soviet Russia are not limited to this. For example, there are cooperative organizations for household chores, hunting, and hairdressing. In particular, agricultural cooperation is also very developed, but its importance is not as great as that of consumer and production cooperation, so this article does not mention it in general.

A Review of the Yarn and Cotton Market in the Past Year (Part 1) Mountain 226

Last year (in 1932), cotton yarn prices were highest in the spring. At that time, due to the invasion of Shanghai by the brutal Japanese, all industries were at a standstill, most yarn factories were shut down, production decreased sharply, standard yarn auctions were suspended one after another, old transactions were all settled and cleared, and the boycott movement was particularly fierce. However, in a corner of South China, there was still demand for spot yarn, but the spot goods on the market were extremely scarce, especially for fine yarn, and prices rose as a result. Therefore, in February and March, the price of 42-count Ren Zhong yarn was 343 taels and 5 qian, the price of 32-count Ren Zhong yarn reached 255 taels, and the price of 20-count Ren Zhong yarn reached a maximum of 188 taels, which was the highest price in recent years. However, how could this situation last? After the armistice agreement was signed and the Japanese army began to withdraw, all yarn factories resumed work, and standard yarn auctions also resumed business on May 2nd. (The standard has been revised to 20-count Ren Zhong from 16-count coarse yarn due to the evolution of the times.) The price on the first day was 154 taels and 5 qian. At that time, due to the financial contraction after the war, the decline of silkworm cocoons, the collapse of the countryside, and the cessation of yarn sales in the interior, coupled with the communist disaster in Jiangxi and Fujian and the banditry in Hubei and Henan, which spread more and more, yarn sales became more and more sluggish. In May and June, the market was still difficult to stabilize and went straight downstream, showing a state of being out of control. The lowest price of standard yarn was 138 taels and 3 qian, and the price of 20-count Ren Zhong yarn (spot goods) was 152 taels, which was a difference of 36 taels compared with the high price in the spring. In July and August, US cotton was affected by humid weather and excessive rainfall, which was not conducive to cotton fields, and the Lausanne Conference Convention was signed, and world commerce was expected to turn around, so the market rose rapidly, from 5 fen to 6 fen. This led to speculative activities. Rongxing Company and Yong'an Factory in this city turned from short to long, with a quota of 26,000 to 27,000 bales. At the same time, in terms of spot yarn, the Guangdong Gang's Mingde Dehao was searching the market very actively, and the standard yarn price rose sharply, from over 138 taels to 147 taels and 148 taels. On August 8th, the US cotton government's estimate was released, and it suddenly rose 85 points (US cotton spot goods) to a maximum of 9.2 cents. With the help of this foreign cotton, the standard yarn price rose irresistibly and reached 158 taels. However, as the market price rose, it hindered actual sales, and Japanese merchants used dumping tactics. Moreover, who would have expected the second US cotton estimate to have an unexpected change, plummeting more than 100 points, causing great shock to the world's people. The standard yarn also plummeted and crashed, and it was unbearable to look back. Gradually after reaching autumn, sales were still depressed. Although the year was abundant, the prices of agricultural products were low, and the lives of farmers were still poor. The accumulated stock of yarn in Shanghai reached more than 110,000 bales, and the market fell further. The buyers also suffered heavy losses. At the end of November, the standard yarn was again 138 taels, which was 3 qian lower than the lowest price in mid-June. In December, cotton rose in price due to the rise in gold prices. The source of cotton was lacking, and the market price rose, which caused the sluggish yarn market to rise by 4 taels to 5 taels. At the end of the year, the war in Sichuan was quelled, and there was some buying for futures. The market situation turned around again. In January, the price even reached 146 taels and 2 qian, and most people predicted that there would be a new atmosphere in the red market this year. Therefore, the market situation became more and more upright. However, the bottom goods are getting thicker every day, foreign aggression is becoming more and more urgent, the economy is drying up, and the world cotton industry is still in decline. The economic situation in Europe and the United States is not optimistic, so what will the future be like? It is not difficult to predict. The following table shows the high and low prices of standard yarn and the monthly delivery prices and total transaction volume throughout the year.

Chun Qiu Ying

Shanghai Chit-Chat 232

— Zhongxian

Rich and Poor

Shanghai is the richest place in China. After years of war, China has gradually absorbed the domestic wealth into the concessions. Roughly speaking, the population in the concessions always increases after each political change. The warlords of China are truly great contributors to the flourishing of the concessions, and they create all opportunities to expand the concessions.

The resident pensioners who can live in Shanghai for a long time are probably families above the middle class. When they come, they bring all their movable property with them. The robbers in Shanghai are really ferocious. It is really unsafe to put foreign money at home, so it is better to deposit it in the bank. To meet so many needs, the banks in Shanghai have suddenly increased.

Apart from the newly opened ones, the existing banks have also added many branches. We see bank branches open everywhere we go. Therefore, some people predict that in the future, banks may even reach the point of setting up stalls.

If banks have more deposits than loans and are constantly paying interest, there is a danger of "swelling to death." Shanghai has money but no one to use it. Is this not a sign of people being rich?

However, opposite the bank stalls, next door, we often find a few small pawnshops with the big character [pawn] on their signs. Although there are many banks, they are still not even one-millionth of the number of small pawnshops. Although the business of banks is good, the business of pawnshops is even better because we know that Shanghai is the richest place, but also the place with the most poor people. In particular, there are many people who are rich in appearance but poor in reality, these people are even worse off than the truly poor.

Changing Location for the Best 233

— Jiang Ping

Where is the Land of Happiness?

These days, because of the aggressive behavior of the expansionists, the residents of Beiping have been leaving in droves, changing location for the best.

Recalling what happened a year ago, how many families were destroyed by the war. The residents of Shanghai thought that they would not suffer this fate. The people of the entire three northeastern provinces were victimized, and the residents of Shanghai thought that they would not follow in their footsteps. But what is the reality? The result is that they suffered the fate and followed in their footsteps. But now, if the residents of Beiping regard the concessions as safety deposit boxes and the interior as the land of happiness, how do they know that they will not repeat the same mistakes in the future? Look, people are advancing step by step, and we are retreating step by step. May I ask, once you have retreated to the coast, where else do you want to retreat to? Therefore, the safety deposit boxes or the land of happiness now may become chopping boards in the future, and we will all become fish and meat?

Therefore, today, the idea of changing location for the best is no longer appropriate, and the mentality of indifference should be eliminated. We cannot willingly make sacrifices, nor can we consider "retreating three times to"

Foreigners Translating Local Gazetteers 234

— Su Kesun

丨What Do Our Countrymen Think?丨

[Know yourself and know your enemy, and you will win every battle.] This seems to have become a mere platitude. However, although we Chinese are fluent in reciting these words, we rarely put them into practice. For example, when studying a certain science, we Chinese only need to go abroad for two years, grasp a bit of superficial knowledge, and immediately return home to act as experts and specialized scholars. If you really delve into it, although their knowledge may not be that profound, their fluent foreign languages are enough to silence you. This phenomenon is evident in the field of science, but whether we have truly achieved the level of "knowing our enemy" in other areas is only known to heaven.

However, foreigners have established churches throughout the interior of our country, even in some villages. Academic exploration teams and scientific investigation teams frequently visit our country several times a year, scouring the mountains and fields. What is the purpose of this? It is simply to "know their enemy."

Recently, a friend from Sichuan sent me a Sichuan newspaper, which contained a piece of news that shocked me: foreigners at the West China University in Chengdu have been using large sums of money to search for many local gazetteers in the old bookstores of Dongyu Street, and have also sent people to various counties to collect them, translate them into foreign languages, and send them back to their home countries. It is said that this work has been going on for a long time. Furthermore, some Chinese students at West China University are willingly acting as foreign slaves and helping with the translation.

What is the reason for foreigners translating our local gazetteers? This reminds me that we often have to go to Japan to translate Chinese literary history. It is especially absurd that Chinese students are helping foreigners translate local gazetteers. No wonder we are helpless when imperialists invade China.

At this time of national crisis, I wonder what our countrymen think when they hear this news?

Dining-ism 235

— Baihe

丨Everyone Should Believe In It丨

In this era of "isms filling the world," we, in this great Republic of China, "dare not lag behind others in isms." All kinds of imported isms are readily available, in every form and variety. Look, capitalists, nationalists, communists, anarchists, fascists, and other ism-ists are as numerous as stars in the sky, making one wonder what they are all about. All these isms have their own principles and reasons, no matter how thoroughly opponents attack them, believers stubbornly uphold them. Being of limited knowledge, I cannot fathom the profound depths of various isms, but after careful consideration, I have invented a "Dining-ism."

What is "Dining-ism"? "Food is the first necessity of the people," as the saying goes. No matter who it is, from the highest-ranking elder to the idle rich, from us literary beggars who live by our pens to the beggars who ask for money, there is no one who can stop eating. Therefore, eating is the most important thing in life. People in ancient times said: "Starving to death is a small matter, losing one's integrity is a big matter." In fact, those who said this were never in danger of starving to death, so they could afford to say such frivolous words. If starving to death were a small matter and eating were not a big problem, then who would be willing to become a robber and risk their life for food?

Honestly, everyone wants to live. To maintain life, besides the air that heaven provides without cost, there is eating. Becoming a traitor, a profiteer, a robber, or a corrupt official, all so-called heinous acts, are ultimately motivated by the need to eat or to obtain the means to eat, in order to sustain life. The goal of capitalists is to solve the problem of eating. The goal of communists is also to solve the problem of eating. Every manufactured or imported ism is ultimately aimed at solving the problem of eating. Therefore, I say that "Dining-ism" is something that everyone, without exception, should believe in and worship. If there is someone who does not acknowledge themselves as a believer in "Dining-ism," then they must be an inhuman monster with supernatural abilities.

Good Policy.

In times of trouble, there is no hope of survival unless we find a way out by confronting the enemy! Friends, we must concentrate our strength, unite ourselves, stand tall, exert our efforts, and move forward together to forge a path to survival from despair! We do not necessarily have to exterminate the Huns, but we must drive them away!

Novel

Hometown 236

— Hu Tiwei

These impressions made Hongye feel even more uneasy than when he had received the letter from his brother. Although the coal-guzzling, black-smoke-spewing monster (the train) tirelessly fulfilled its "extra fast" mission, Hongye was still dissatisfied, wishing he could step directly into C Village and see his father's thin cheeks and white-haired forehead. But reality did not allow it, and with a whistle, he finally disappeared with a group of laughing young men and women into a small hotel near the station.

As soon as his head hit the pillow, a group of what Shanghai people call "rich bugs" lined up to greet him, and he had to struggle to open his drowsy eyes and do his best to deal with them. It is said that "rich bugs" are a special product of the metropolis of Shanghai. C Village is rarely found. It seems that C Village is lucky to be connected to the land of wealth by train, so they also enjoy the privilege of being stationed here. After fighting for a while, he felt that he really could not resist and it was better to be polite and let them invade. Suddenly, a figure flashed in front of the bed, and Hongye jumped up!

"Sir, do you want to call someone to play with?"

"Get out! Lock the door for me!"

"This kind of thing is even more sinful than rich bugs and should also be killed," Hongye thought angrily, and got up to lock the door.

When he woke up the second time, he didn't know what time it was. There was a banging and knocking outside the door!

"Who is it? What's the matter?"

"Sir, open the door. Room inspection."

Hongye opened the door, and the bellboy he had previously seen was leading four imposing policemen. The one in front was holding a circulation book.

"What is your surname? What is your name? Where are you from? Where are you going?"

He asked four questions and then waved his hand and left. Hongye looked at the watch beside his pillow, and it was exactly 2:15. He was even more angry. Is this protecting public security or disturbing travelers? Suddenly, a thought flashed through his mind and he understood. Ah! Perhaps this is a small retribution for my reluctance to spend money to call someone.

During this short journey, since the Creator was unwilling to grant him a sweet dream, he no longer lingered. In the dim dawn, he continued his journey on the yellow train to C Village. After crossing the C River, where sandy sails and a crescent moon remained, he hurriedly boarded the first long-distance bus. He remembered that he often saw news in the newspaper about accidents involving long-distance buses in C Village, causing injuries and deaths. Either the bus overturned into a rice field, or it jumped into the river. It is said that the drivers on this provincial highway all have a touch of official air. Being called "drivers" (駕駛員) rather than the "motorcar drivers" (汽車夫) that people in Shanghai mention, of course, has a distinction. First, they do not want "tips" (克門沙). If a guest gives them a tip, not only will they not accept it, but they will be offended and consider it a malicious insult! This refers to a chartered car hired by an individual, which costs eight yuan and eight jiao. (2)

Children's Paradise

Cars and Turtles 237

— Huaji

"The shape of a car and the appearance of a turtle are very similar." This was advocated by William Stout, a famous American design expert. Because the shape of a turtle is a "parabola," a streamlined body can reduce air resistance. No matter how strong the wind blows against the turtle, it can move quickly. Cars also need to reduce the air resistance they face when traveling on the ground, so they should be manufactured according to the shape of a turtle.

(1) When the wind blows towards the turtle

(2) When the wind blows towards the car

Then, the turtle can be said to be a model for automobiles. As the saying goes, when a turtle races against a rabbit, the rabbit cannot catch up with the turtle. This is because it has no air resistance. Recently, scientists, based on this principle, have also imitated the shape of turtles when manufacturing bullets. This is to reduce air resistance during launch, so that it can shoot very far. If you look at the diagram above, you will naturally understand.

— Bingyu

Student: "Teacher, the wings of an airplane are the same as those of a bird."

Teacher: "The invention of the airplane originally came from the idea of how birds can fly."

Student: "But the actions of an airplane are not as natural as those of a bird. First, birds can fly back and forth in the air without falling, but airplanes often fall. Second, birds can dive into the water and stand on branches, but airplanes cannot."

Wang Er's mother, because she had to go out, told Wang Ke to stay home and watch the house. She said: "When someone comes, no matter who it is, you can say that your mother is not at home, and I don't know anything."

Dynamization of Food 239

The food we eat every day provides us with the energy for activity when we are young. How exactly does this happen? This is what we should understand. Because the food we eat every day can help our bodies develop. But after a day of exercise [which is what it means to live a day], we also consume a considerable amount of energy. (Our daily activity requires about 2,000 calories.) The dynamization of food is explained below:

Rice | One bowl, weighing about 150 grams, has about 220 calories, which can raise a weight 120 feet high.

Tofu | One block, weighing about 200 grams, has about 120 calories, which can raise a weight 72 feet high.

Egg | One, weighing about 60 grams, has about 96 calories, which can raise a weight about 65 feet high.

Milk | One 合 (gé, a unit of volume, about 180 ml), weighing about 185 grams, has about 130 calories, which can raise a weight 73 feet high.

Peanuts | 100 grams, has about 590 calories, which can raise a weight 324 feet high.

Beef | 100 grams, has about 130 calories, which can raise a weight 78 feet high.

Free Talk

Divergent Paths (II) 240

— Tizhi

"Old Zhou! You are really too busy. Fortunately, your body is still strong; otherwise, others would not be able to handle it."

"Alas! My body is getting weaker every year. Recently, I often feel dizzy and have back pain. I want to take some medicine, but I don't have the money. Just think, this monthly salary of thirty yuan has to cover my own food, clothing, and the living expenses of my parents, wife, and children. I am always in poverty and labor, how can I not get sick!" Old Zhou's voice trembled a little.

I couldn't think of any appropriate words to comfort him for a moment, so we both kept silent for the time being. Quietly listening to the mournful sound of the rain outside the window, it increased the sorrow in our hearts.

"Didn't you say a few days ago that you were going to Haimen? The treatment there should be better, right? Have you received a letter?" My thoughts turned to his letter again.

"Yes, I received a letter from a friend today. He said that the school authorities there dare not hire people with socialist ideas."

"Do they know that you have socialist ideas? The standard for hiring teachers is really too bizarre; ideas are kept in each person's mind, who can prove who has them or not? It's really exhausting!" I couldn't help but feel a little angry when I heard this strange information!

"Even if they hire me, I won't go. The school authorities like that must be fools."

"Yes! The oppression of the spirit and the oppression of matter are equally unbearable for us!"

"I would rather suffer the oppression of matter." Old Zhou resolutely expressed his attitude towards dealing with reality.

"Then what are you going to do?" I asked him urgently about his plan.

"I'm not going to teach anymore; I'm going to become an outlaw." He raised his head, his attitude was very firm!

"Become an outlaw? Become an outlaw?" I was stunned, but at the same time, I seemed to have received an unexpected revelation.

"Yes, become an outlaw! Only by becoming an outlaw!" As Old Zhou said this, his eyes closed tightly again, and his lips flickered slightly.

I didn't want to ask him any further, so I quietly walked out.

The night outside the door was as silent as death, without a single ray of light, only the sound of dripping rain and whistling wind could be heard. (The End)

One Year After the Bloody Battle 241

— Xuan

If the "September 18th Incident" in Shenyang was like a bolt from the blue, then the bloody battle in Shanghai on "January 28th" was like a storm? Now it has been a year since "January 28th," and the whole of China is still in the dark and suffocating atmosphere before the storm, and the whole world is stepping up its arms, waiting for an opportunity to break out. The god of war is grinning!

We recall the Shanghai bloody battle at that time, the great fire burned down the prosperous Zhabei, the shells swept the Jiangwan and Wusong training grounds, the wounded soldiers and refugees in the concessions were crammed everywhere, the capitalists worried about government bonds and coupons turning into waste paper, worried about the forever falling land prices in Zhabei, the small merchants in the interior frowned because Shanghai "money houses were not connected," and the farmers along the railway line painfully watched their fields being encircled as airfields, and trenches being dug. But what is Shanghai like a year later? The Northeast Refugee Relief Art Exhibition closed in the cheers of "Flower Selection." Department stores with big discounts are crowded with customers. Dr. Mei came to Shanghai to perform, and many people couldn't get tickets. Newly made short coats and newly made even longer cheongsams: The bustling Shanghai is still so bustling!! No, even more bustling! If it weren't for the gossipy newspapers frequently reporting that Jehol was in critical condition and that artillery fire was heard at Shanhaiguan, who would believe that our national crisis is still not over, that I do not offend others, but others offend me, and that the so-called "long-term resistance" is actually "long-term" [not] resistance!

Shanghai is really a peaceful world, but the Shanghai petty bourgeoisie who are kept in the dark have not forgotten the lessons of this day last year. Seeing that the Japanese Marine Corps in Hongkou is going to hold a "review," they are once again panicked and moving one after another. Respectable and pitiful petty bourgeoisie! Don't panic! Haven't you heard that Britain and France have a secret agreement with Japan that Japan will no longer harass Shanghai, and that the exchange condition is that Britain and France tacitly allow Japan's military actions in Jehol and Yuguan? The rich are much smarter than you, they know that Shanghai is a peaceful world.

Don't you see them singing and dancing every day and night?

Device for Examining the Authenticity of Ancient Art 244

— Liu

Ancient works of art are loved and appreciated by everyone, but because of certain motives, some people often betray their conscience and create many fakes, attempting to achieve their goals.

Many scientists have seen this phenomenon and deeply feel that the research on the authenticity of ancient art is urgently needed. So everyone came to study, and recently a satisfactory result has been obtained. The inventor is Mr. A.P.L. Laurie, a member of the Royal Society of Arts in England. This device uses ultraviolet light, and its shape is like an ordinary camera, making it very convenient to carry. No matter what character or painting, after being examined by it, the skills and colors of the character or painting itself can be seen, none of which can be seen by the naked eye. England has already applied this device, but other countries do not yet have it. Speaking of China, no one is studying ultraviolet light, so it is even more impossible to talk about it.

The Shanghai Local Supplement of Shen Bao

Casual Talk

On Saving the Nation 246

— I

Speaking of it, I find myself amusing. Last time I discussed selling the nation, and now I'm talking about saving it. Can a nation truly be both sold and saved? However, upon careful consideration, it's not entirely without reason. Many people are eternally infamous for selling their country, while many others are celebrated for saving it. Just as there was a Qin Hui, there had to be a Yue Fei. And Yue Fei's thinking became more evident because of Qin Hui.

There are many precedents, so why list them all? Therefore, my argument is not entirely without basis.

So, how can this nation be saved? I say: There are many ways to save the nation, it just depends on how you choose and implement them. Broadly speaking, [declarations] [telegrams] can save the nation, [Buddhist rituals] [religious ceremonies] can save the nation, [protests] [written opinions] can save the nation, [non-resistance] can save the nation, [resistance] with a vow of [long-term war] can even better save the nation, and even [the Analects] [the Doctrine of the Mean] can save the nation. On a smaller scale, [National Arts Save the Nation], [Art Saves the Nation], [fundraising] can save the nation, [opium] smoking can also save the nation, [dancing] can save the nation, and [entertainments] can even better save the nation. By extension, eating can save the nation, dressing can save the nation, sleeping, shitting, nothing is impossible to save the nation. However, when eating, you must change to eating [foreign wheat] bread; when dressing, you must wear [genuine domestic goods]; when sleeping, you must [sleep with a spear as your pillow] and [taste gall]; and when shitting, you must use a flushing toilet, otherwise, it will lose the meaning of saving the nation and will not achieve the effect of saving the nation.

How great and flourishing, how mighty and magnificent, are the ways to save the nation!

Someone might ask: "These ways of saving the nation have been practiced in our country for a long time, so why hasn't China been saved yet?" I say: This gentleman is mistaken. China has not yet perished, if people didn't exert efforts to save it, how could it be like this? And are the achievements of these great ways shallow? Moreover, it has only lost the three northeastern provinces, how can it be considered perished? Since the nation has not perished, then why save it?

Someone might say, "[The nation] should be saved when it is not yet perished." Therefore, the point returns to the beginning, China must be saved, there is no doubt. Furthermore, the whole country is bustling with everyone talking about saving the nation, and I, with my [patriotism, dare not lag behind others], how could I willingly stay behind in saving the nation? Therefore, when all of you are having tea and meals, it is perfectly acceptable to talk about saving the nation. However, it is not really necessary to truly put [effective] methods into practice, because at this time there are so many people selling the nation in China. Why must you imitate Yue Fei and put in effort?

However, the only ones who can truly save the nation are those Pullman porters, because only they can feel the pain of national subjugation.

Common Sense

Common Sense on Using Fountain Pens 247

— Gu Lushuang

In the business, academic, and political worlds, almost everyone has a fountain pen. It is truly because it is convenient and also aesthetically pleasing. Therefore, even though the value is very significant, the public is willing to buy one. The pen is bought, but people don't know how to protect it. A pen that was bought in good condition soon has all kinds of problems after not much use. The wealthy go and buy another one, but those with slightly less financial leeway can only use that broken pen, blaming the pen for being bad, not knowing that they ruined it themselves. Therefore, I will record the common sense of using fountain pens to tell the readers.

There are many brands of ink on the market, and their compositions are different. Therefore, for a certain pen, which ink to use should not be changed. Otherwise, due to the chemical reaction of the two inks, the nib or the rubber tube will be damaged. If it is necessary to switch, it is advisable to wash away the old ink before filling with the new ink.

It is advisable to use high-quality ink. Inferior ink is prone to precipitation, which will block the pen tube. The ink bottle should always be tightly capped, otherwise even high-quality ink will precipitate. Users must be aware of this. Among domestic inks, the Dahua brand and the Standard brand are worth using and are not inferior to Waterman and Parker.

If the ink gathers at the nib when using the pen, or if the ink drips down from time to time, this is evidence that the ink in the rubber tube has run out. Therefore, the tube is filled with air, causing the pressure to increase, and the ink is forced down. If the ink is filled, this problem can be avoided, so don't panic.

If the ink cannot flow down, the pen can be washed with cold water, using the same method as filling the ink. The nib must be washed with cold water. Hot water will damage the color of the pen barrel and cause the rubber tube to rupture easily.

When the fountain pen is pulled out of the pen cap, if the pen barrel is covered with ink, then the two small holes on the pen cap must be cleared with a needle. This is because the small holes are blocked, the air is not circulating, the pressure outside the pen is small, and the ink can flow out.

The above are all common knowledge that pen users should know. If you follow this, a pen can be used for at least several years.

Eye-Sore Thatched Houses 248

— Hongshui

After several days of snow, the sunlight has now melted it, turning this place into a muddy, unbearable road. Walking on it, boots are almost completely immersed in the mud. If one is not careful, one will be sent tumbling back. Originally, few people paid attention to it, perhaps because it was far from the city.

At dusk, A Gen, as usual, returned home from the factory. He put down his small basket and ran to the garden behind the thatched house to help his mother plant vegetables and water them, and to carry the loads for his mother. However, now he lost his usual calmness and could no longer live his usual leisurely life: the door was tightly closed, and through the straw cracks, he could faintly hear bursts of sobbing. He was terribly frightened!

The next day, the east had just revealed the fish-belly white of dawn. A Gen lazily got up, silently thinking in his heart: "Mother is freezing and sick, and no one is taking care of her. How can I have the courage to go to work? Alas! As a son, I should stay by her side and fulfill my filial duties." Therefore, he felt the sadness of being uncared for, and he also recalled the joy of his father's presence! In an instant, the factory whistle continued to sound, sound, sound. This was the last warning. For the sake of the bread problem, he had to go away reluctantly.

The atmosphere in the thatched house was extremely quiet. Apart from the faint throbbing sound of A Gen's mother's heart, it was simply impossible to find anything to describe.

"Open the door... open... open." Suddenly, someone outside was hitting the bamboo fence door and shouting.

"See if your man speaks," a policeman in black uniform stared at A Gen's mother and asked.

"Sir, my husband died long ago. I only have a fourteen-year-old son, and I have no other relatives."

Page 20

"Call his son here, don't be so long-winded with her." Another policeman said.

"Sir, what, what, what's the matter? My son is in the factory! Discuss things with me."

"Hmm? You are ordered to completely move out of your house today, and all the nearby thatched houses will be demolished."

"Why, why..." She asked anxiously, her voice trembling, but before she could finish her words, she heard two more words in her ear:

"What? Demolish the thatched houses!" It was a majestic and arrogant policeman shouting.

"Great Lord, have mercy, how can we move? I'm still sick."

"Heh, sick? What a joke."

"Sick, in pain." She said: "We are hardworking commoners. Since the outbreak of the Shanghai War, everyone has taken refuge here. It took almost a year of hard work to build this thatched house. If you tear it down for us, where can we go? Besides, if our house had not been destroyed in Zhabei, then why would we be so unlucky?"

"Too much talk? Immediately move... move... move." At the same time, two crisp slaps were imprinted on her cheeks. "Alas! We are not thieves, not kidnappers, why are you forcing us to have no way to make a living? Anyway, I'll offer you my old life..." She couldn't help but shed a few lines of bitter tears, and fainted in the mud.

"Get up, old woman! This is the order of the ×× Bureau, and it really cannot be accommodated. Hurry up, or we will have to do it ourselves." A more amiable policeman advised.

"Sir, what reason does the bureau have for demolishing our thatched houses and forcing us to move immediately?"

"That's right, because the thatched houses and fences [are an eyesore to the city]!"

"Huh? The old woman doesn't seem to care at all, she's really crazy, take her to the bureau." The majestic and arrogant policeman interjected.

Dusk shrouded the earth. A Gen, responding to the factory whistle, ran home with hope, only to find piles of straw and bamboo fences scattered miserably on the ground under his wooden-eyed gaze. He could no longer find his loving mother or the thatched house that could keep out the cold!

Staff Correspondence

Inheritance Problem 251

Editor:

I am naturally stubborn and indecisive when encountering matters. Now, because of an inheritance problem, I am indecisive. I will state the detailed situation as follows: I hope for clear instructions, and I am extremely eager for them.

My family is poor. My third uncle is over sixty years old. He has been working away from home for many years and has accumulated considerable wealth. However, he has no children of his own. Early in his life, he proposed to adopt me as his son, but it did not come to fruition. In the eighteenth year of the Republic of China (1929), he adopted the second son of my eldest uncle as his heir. Unexpectedly, he did not cherish himself and spent his days chasing after women. My third uncle repeatedly admonished him, but the speaker was earnest and the listener was indifferent. My third uncle's heart changed because of this, and finally, in August of last year, the two sides broke up, and my third uncle drove him out. In December, my third uncle came to Shanghai to visit and intended to reaffirm his previous proposal to make me his heir. Of course, I am happy to comply with this, but I am afraid that the expelled cousin will be unwilling and will inevitably get into endless lawsuits in the future. Therefore, I am indecisive. (Remainder omitted.) Respectfully, Yan Xiangwen.

Editor's Note: Article 1143 of the Inheritance Chapter of the Civil Code stipulates that "If there are no direct descendants, an inheritor may be designated in a will for all or part of his property, but only to the extent that it does not violate the provisions regarding special reserved portions." Therefore, Yan Jun's third uncle can, of course, freely designate anyone as the heir to his property. However, because there is a factual event of raising Yan Jun's cousin in the past, in order to avoid future troubles, the procedures must be perfect. For the plan now, Yan Jun's third uncle should quickly register the termination of inheritance (referring to Yan Jun's cousin) and the establishment of inheritance (referring to Yan Jun). This type of registration can be done with the local self-government organization. If this system of personal registration has not yet been implemented in Yan Jun's hometown, then he can also apply to the court or the county government that also handles judicial affairs for filing. At the same time, a will should be made. According to our opinion, this will should adopt a "notarized will" to be appropriate.

The above is just a way to solve this problem from a legal standpoint. We believe that enjoying [the blessing of inheritance] is something that a righteous man should consider shameful. If Yan Jun's third uncle insists on making Yan Jun his heir, in order to comfort the old man, of course, he cannot refuse. But do not think of this as an opportunity to make a fortune! Yan Jun should try to guide his cousin to the right path. Turning back is the shore, turning away from evil and returning to righteousness is extremely easy after receiving a great stimulus (being expelled). At that time, Yan Jun should intercede on his behalf before his third uncle and restore their relationship. Half of the third uncle's property may as well be inherited by each. This will not disappoint the elderly now, and it will also preserve the feelings of the brothers, and you will not lose considerable benefits yourself. This is the most appropriate and noblest way.

Finally, because it is still unknown whether Yan Jun's cousin will be determined to be good, we believe that legal procedures should still be completed as soon as possible so that you can control your rights. This is what we mean by having a foolproof plan!

Now my mistress has a son, although not born from my wife, it is still the blood of the Xia family. She must be happy to hear it. Who knew that when she heard the news, her face turned ashen, her eyes rolled up, and with a [thud] she passed out! After several hours, she slowly called her wandering soul back. From then on, this matter could not be mentioned again. Mentioning it to her would make her pass out for half a day, really like a death warrant. So my fear of my wife is not because I am afraid of her being too fierce, but because I am afraid of her body being too delicate and too prone to passing out!"

"Children's love is long, heroes' energy is short," all men who cannot withstand the play of women use this idiom as an excuse. Zhongnan succumbed to the skirt because he was afraid that his wife would pass out. Someone modified this idiom after presenting it to the couple: [The master's love is long, the mistress's energy is short].

Film Supplement

Monday, January 23, 1933, Republic of China (Not separately published)

The Economic Crisis in Hollywood 254

— Fulun

In this publication and other film publications, the wealth and extravagance of Hollywood seem to be happily talked about, so the impression given to readers is that it is paved with gold, the walls are made of white jade, and silver-gray limousines float around silently, inside which sit the deities of paradise. In reality, however, it is no longer like that. Therefore, in order to dispel readers' excessive admiration, it is necessary to introduce this article.

Hollywood news reporter Ms. Ningna Punam said that the content of Hollywood has an inscrutable core, but the exterior still tries to maintain the scene, unwilling to collapse. A certain French film critic also issued a shocking prediction a few days ago, saying that within six months, Hollywood would still experience a major economic and artistic collapse that could shock the world. Although we cannot be certain that Hollywood will collapse in the next six months, we can at least say that this premonition is [not without cause].

Ms. Ningna once visited a big star in Hollywood. He still lived in the most luxurious house on Beaver Hill. When she went inside, it was time for the hosts to dine. She saw that the food on the table did not seem very rich, but she still didn't pay much attention. Later, she saw that there were no electric lights in the house, and they were burning candles. She slowly became a little suspicious. But the host said that his wife didn't like tranquility, so he didn't turn on the electric lights. Later, she took advantage of a moment when the host wasn't paying attention and sneaked into another room, turned on the electric switch, but there was no electricity. She suddenly understood and felt a kind of creepy fear. Ah, the economic recession has actually invaded this golden-cage, nightless singing and dancing film city! She also snuck into the cellar (underground level, specially for coal stoves, pots, and cooking places), struck a match, and found that there was no gas on the gas stove either. She discovered many things: in this big star's house, not only had the electric lights and gas been cut off, but even the telephone was disconnected.

But he still had to live in this big house, tough it out, and still had to ride in a luxurious car. When people asked, "How are you?" he still had to put on a brave face and say, "Very well, thank you." Because if he didn't do so, he would immediately be looked down upon and would not be able to stand, so he would have to pack up his bags and scram.

Of course, he was not the only one affected in the same way. Many banks closed, various investments failed, and the stars who used to have solid icebergs to rely on were now penniless. In the past, they could lose their temper with the factory owners and directors, quit whenever they wanted, but now they had to humbly seek any job to do. Many had nothing to do this year, but they refused to admit unemployment and had to sit in their cars every day and stop at the door of big companies, or turn around in the photography studios. Sigh, how bitter and pitiful this is!

Overseas News

Two New Inventions in the Film Industry 255

— Xingzhi

Recently, a large theater has been newly built in California, USA. It is composed of two theaters, with the stage in the middle. When the show starts, both sides can enter and watch. In this way, the seats can be more spacious and not too crowded. It can also be regarded as a novel idea to use one stage to perform the functions of two theaters. The inventor is an American engineer who planned for a long time before realizing it.

A professor at a technical university in Germany has invented an optical device that can be used in theaters to write words on the glass screen of this machine while the movie is playing, and the words will be projected onto the screen. This provides various conveniences for reporting temporary news, current events, and important news, and celebrity autographs. At the beginning of the invention, this professor was interested in teaching extremely complex formulas in mathematics in a large classroom, and it was later used in theaters. Now many theaters have adopted it.

"Star" Company's New Production Plan 256

— Qingxia

Although the Star Company's studio doesn't have as many as Lianhua, the total number of productions last year seems to be no less than Lianhua. However, before shooting each film, they do not limit the maximum number of feet of film to be used. For example, [A Laughing Tale of Love]; [The Flower of Freedom]; etc., all used more than 30,000 feet of film to obtain about 10,000 feet of film. A seven- or eight-thousand-foot film using more than 20,000 feet of film is even a majority of their productions. Therefore, the total number of films they use each year always exceeds that of any other company. They feel that this is not a good strategy in the long run and want to implement savings immediately; however, in order to make the productions perfect, they finally dare not implement it suddenly. This also makes them extremely difficult.

Recently, Zheng Zhengqiu once discussed improvement measures with important employees of the company such as Zhou Jianyun because of this problem. At that time, it was decided to shorten the length of the film and increase the shooting of [cartoons]. Famous painters Wan Laiming and Wan Guchan were hired by Star to serve as the director of [cartoons].

[The Mysterious Little Detective] is the [cartoon] that has just started shooting, with actors such as Yi Zhiyuan and Zhang Min; the length of the film is one thousand feet. Because Star's productions will be shorter than in the past, this kind of [cartoon] is prepared to be shown with the feature film in the future.

Currently in the Chinese film industry, the lack of child stars and the urgency of the demand is a fact that no one can deny. Therefore, this group of female child stars nurtured at Tianyi Film Company is truly worthy of our attention! Here, the reporter specifically introduces this group of female child stars:

Yuan Meiyun: Before engaging in film work, she was a famous little female stage performer. She has a petite and exquisite figure, a lively and clever demeanor, and is even more richly endowed with acting talent. In the current Chinese film industry, she can be considered the number one female child star!

She is innocent and naive, can sing and play the piano, like a lively little bird. In the silent film era, she had already played important roles in many films. She also participated in the talkies "Amusement Fair," "Battlefield," and "Orphan Girl." In the new film "Double Mandarin Ducks in a Sea of Sin," she plays the daughter of a wealthy man raised by poor people, and her performance is excellent.

Chen Qixia: She is the younger sister of Chen Yumei, the boss's wife of Tianyi Film Company.
