Chen Jingfang: Although she is young, she has already grown as fresh and beautiful as a lotus flower. She played a maid in "Traces of Orchid Valley" and received good reviews. Some even said that her success was no less than Chen Yanyan's in "A Cut Plum." We hope that she will work harder in the future and become a famous child star.

Joan Crawford's Makeup Alert 258

Joan Crawford, Greta Garbo, and Norma Shearer are the three major pillars of MGM. Because each person has their own art and their own audience, they are constantly moving forward, wanting to seize the throne of MGM. Greta Garbo relied on her mysterious charm and finally seized this throne. Therefore, the ambitious Joan Crawford engaged in fierce competition against Garbo, wanting to snatch the throne from Garbo's hands. Now that Garbo has returned to her native Sweden, the throne of MGM has also been taken by Joan Crawford. However, the audience's support for Garbo has not diminished because of this. Our clever Joan Crawford wants to turn the audience's support for Garbo to support her. This can only be done by imitating Garbo. Therefore, she has recently imitated Garbo in her makeup, wanting to win the audience's favor. We are waiting to see in her upcoming film "Rain" (The Rain), we can see that her makeup is a bit mysterious. Those two thick lips are truly sensual enough, but although she dresses up like this, she is very concerned about the audience's criticism of her change in style, fearing that the audience will have a negative reaction to her makeup and lose her throne. Therefore, she has recently been very concerned about the audience's psychology.

Film and Literary Taste 259

— Huang Zhenxia

(II) Good Night, Vienna

The customs of 19th century Central Europe, the culture of 19th century Central Europe.

Vienna, this German-Austrian national capital, is encircled by the blue Danube River. In the early 19th century, ancient castles were heavily guarded, and the melody of waltzes floated lightly on the fine grass. It is the oldest city in Central Europe, the imperial capital of the Holy Roman Empire, the cradle of genius musicians, and the center of Romantic sentiment. The classical beauties we see in famous paintings, with long skirts sweeping the ground and a large black mole on their faces, as well as the knights with precious swords and steeds, the so-called German Blue Cross Knights, the spirit of chivalry, crystallized into this medieval Romantic culture, and Beethoven and Schubert and others transformed its atmosphere with the sounds of paradise. Even in modern times, its position in European art still occupies the most excellent position. "Good Night, Vienna," is a musical comedy set against this "City of Dreams." The so-called "Good Night, Vienna" is a modern knight's farewell call to this "City of Dreams" on his journey. Its poignant emotion is actually the same as Byron's "Good Night, My Native Land" when he bid farewell to England. The structure of the whole film is rich in interest and extremely warm and beautiful, and can be called a by-product of the essence of Western musical art. Its attitude towards life is a lively satire against solemnity, but it still does not escape the Romantic style of medieval knights and maidens, such as the male lead must be a military officer, and the female lead must first be a flower girl and then a famous actress.

In short, the film highlights the beauty of Vienna's dream and its beautiful characters. This is purely a by-product of literature and art, a condiment against turning life into a solemn and serious affair, with a bit of Parisian humor. If viewed from a trendy political perspective, since Vienna is the birthplace of European feudal forces, and the characters in the play are all extremely petty-bourgeois inferiorized, without the slightest revolution, it is naturally just a "poisonous anesthetic."

Introducing the Fairy in Rainbow Garments 260

— Luo Ba Gao

The German Ufa Film Company occupies a transcendent position in the world film scene. Its productions, no matter what kind of subject matter, are all focused and fully committed, without the slightest compromise. From its "Slaying the Dragon and Encountering the Immortal" all the way to the "Dragon and Phoenix Dance" currently showing at the Nanjing Grand Theater, which one has not given the audience a wonderful and good impression while meeting the conditions suitable for film art?

It is said that "Fairy in Rainbow Garments" is a superior product of Ufa Company last year, on par with "Dragon and Phoenix Dance." In major European cities, it enjoys the same fame. "Dragon and Phoenix Dance" is a musical opera, and "Fairy in Rainbow Garments" is also a musical opera, but the subject matter is different, and the director's methods are different. In addition, the script of "Fairy in Rainbow Garments" is humorous, a small satire on life.

The depiction of the whole play is very light, cold, and has a Parisian style. It is very humorous to make fun of a small country. However, it writes about a dreamlike life, happy and sweet, succumbing to the supremacy of love, becoming the yearning of young men and women.

Its theme is to use the small to symbolize the big. It has absolute doubts about the monarchy. It satirizes bureaucratic politicians and soldiers. It rebukes wealthy merchants and magnates. It ridicules subordinate staff, but it sympathizes with the burning of the fire of life and the activity of youth.

Its English name Ronny will be released at the New Light Theater soon.

The Achievements of "Si Lang Visits His Mother" 261

— Zhao Hu

The entire "Si Lang Visits His Mother," produced by Ancient Sound Film Company, directed by Yin Shengtao, and starring the famous actors Xue Yanqin and Tan Fuying, has been completed. Xue Yanqin and Tan Fuying are both famous actors on the stage. This is their first time shooting a talkie, and their performance is as good as seasoned movie stars, which is truly rare and commendable.

At the beginning of the filming of the film. They took great pains for the scenery in the play, especially the magnificent imperial palace garden of the Empress Dowager Xiao, which is not often seen by the audience.

"Si Lang Visits His Mother" is indeed more wonderful on the screen than on the stage, because there is a great background to embellish it. In terms of the number of people and horses alone, it is several times more than on the stage, so the "Si Lang Visits His Mother" on the screen is enough to satisfy the audience.

A Scene from "Si Lang Visits His Mother" 262

The Story of "The Match King" (17) 263

— Translated by Xi Meng

Here, he created his own hell, but it was also here that he himself fell into the hell he created, and perished with the others who had fallen into this hell before him.

The Italian treasury bond was forged and has now been discovered. The transfer of 40 million yuan has also been cancelled. Dark clouds are gathering from all sides, and the net is closing down. Paul Kreuger, Eric, and all other colleagues cannot escape, and their reputations are ruined. The doors of the prison are opened wide, waiting for their arrival.

New York, London, Berlin, Paris, exchanges all over the world are tottering and about to fall, making earth-shattering sounds. The cabinets of many countries have fallen, and the governments of many countries have been overthrown. Revolutions are happening everywhere. People are panicked and cannot live in peace.

Paul returned to the office and heard the curses of the people. He truly had no way to go to heaven and no door to enter the earth, so he quietly fled. He sat alone at his desk, thinking that he admitted that this failure was inescapable. He suddenly had a surge of emotion.

All his past experiences came back to his mind one by one, swirling rapidly like a whirlpool, like scenes in a movie, reappearing before his eyes.

Like a novel, the cause and effect are intertwined, and he already knew the outcome in his heart, with no way to escape.

Finally, he opened his secret safe and took out a pistol and put it in his pocket. He quickly left his office and walked to the balcony. He thought of the past events one after another, starting with Qing Shoufu, who was squeezed out of his job in Chicago, USA, all the way to Murna telling him that she had already loved someone else 丨丨 those people who had been harmed by him, one by one stood before him 丨丨 Bei Bei, Sanya, Lodinsky, the old inventor, Scalatti, bankers, politicians, financiers from various countries... A terrifying ferocity suddenly flashed in his eyes. He raised his gun and pointed it at his own temple. In the hazy darkness, only a flash of orange-yellow light was seen, and he had already rolled over the railing from the balcony and fallen onto the street.

Many people heard the gunshot and chased to his office, from the office to the balcony. They looked down and were all stunned. Everyone desperately ran towards the elevator.

On the street downstairs, they saw his body, and each person had their own thoughts.

Paul's body was lying in the gutter, his head hitting the wheel of a scavenger's two-wheeled cart. Next to his heels, there was a pile of burnt matches. Eric finally said to himself:

[He came from digging in the gutter, 丨丨 he rose from the gutter all the way to controlling the world 丨丨 he still died in the gutter.]

(The End)
